電影專刊

美國的電影刋物是否盡是公司或明星們的宣傳工具？ 136

— 密齊

（一）是的方面（上）

美國的電影刋物，卽以雜誌一類而言，共有二十二種。它們的銷數，最小的有十二萬六千，最大的有五十六萬五千。我數須要知道，美國的報紙雜誌，差不多它們的銷數，都是由一個銷數調查會檢定，而不能虚報的。因此，以二十幾種電影雜誌的銷數，合計起來，就形成了美國社會生活的一個生要部份，並且亦是美國文化的一面了。統計起來，每個月化一角二角錢去買些電影雜誌看的，一共八百八十萬人，倘若我們拿普通兩三個人看一本電影，這還是最低的統計，我們就可以知道每一個月看電影雜誌的人，總有二三百萬之譜。而它們的勢力，亦就很可觀了。

現在有人說，這些電影雜誌，都是好萊塢的忠僕，雇用的宣傳者，明星們的工具，它們掩飾了影城裏無數的罪惡，并且煽熾了那種性慾狂的影業，在美國社會上的勢力。好萊塢影戲生活，以及明星們的地位，都被他們描寫得金碧輝煌，不可迫視，而惟一的功用，不過是代影片公司作喉舌，替它們推廣銷路而已。

以上係一般人對於電影刋物進攻的開花彈。要證明以上的話的成立，他們又將這種雜誌的内容，考核了一下。他們發現了在這些雜誌裏面，有許多不實不盡的地方。第一就是道聽途說的Ｇossip。他們說這Ｇossip已經成了電影雜誌的中心成份。第一家雜誌所登載的，都是儘量的無稽空談，而没有一家肯尋求宣佈好萊塢的眞實景况的。照電影雜誌上所登載的看起來，好萊塢是美國惟一的樂園，世界上的天堂。差不多每一本雜誌，都有無稽空談的一欄的。它們都有它們的華爾德温吉爾（ＷalterＷinchelI好萊塢的一位名記者）。他們是無所不知，無所不曉的人；它們能鑽到每個人的心裏，每個人的家裏，去刺探新聞，以致一段新聞，神仙還没有曉得之前，他們已經知道了。這不是太渺茫無稽了嗎？

除掉了短篇的無稽空談之外，還有許多長文。這種長文那裏來的？它們卽使不是影片公司或電影明星，寫好了交給雜誌登載的，亦必是由關係方面授意發表的。它們的内容，亦是空虚得很，並無實質新聞。它們大都是根據於一個明星的Ｇossip發　鼓吹起來的。要是有一個聰明人去設法訪查一下，他就可以發現，每一次一段長文關於一個明星的生活，發表之後，接連着必登有一張影片公映，而那個受宣傳的明星，亦就是那張影片的主角。我們需要知道這種電影雜誌的編輯部，都是和廣告部通同一氣。無分彼此的。所以這些文章亦都是爲一張影片或一個明星而發的瞎吹瞎擂。它們爲了自身的收入起見，就心甘情願的爲公司當局利用了，去愚弄社會上的一般人。（未完）

影片談評

評「愛斯基摩」 137

— 凌鶴

Eskimo丨大光明丨

當我們在一連羅曼主義的戀愛把戲的美國影片之淫靡的空氣中，偶然發現了這一「愛斯基摩」之後，我們亟應禮讚這一位作者W·S·范達克。不消說。我們應當給與這作品極高的評價。

爲了使讀者諸君對於他易於明瞭起見。在此約略的介紹。他於一九二七年，在南海攝製了一部「“WheteShadowintheSouthSea”」，一九二九年深入菲洲腹地攝製了「TraderHorn」，這是我們永遠不會忘懷的。至於這一影片，乃一九三三年在北冰洋所作。無疑的，這是一部偉大的作品。

先從故事的結構說起，在此可看出思想之一斑。

首先，我們所要知道的是他爲什麽要以北冰洋作背景？這固然是因着冰山雪地的奇景，可作爲銀幕上的奇觀，而我們現在所要注意的，却是他如何採取素材以及如何處理題材，在這中間我們便可認識他的世界觀了。

「愛斯基摩」除了介紹了當地土人的生活和習慣之外，更展開了他們的純樸與勇敢的性格。他們是原始的生活着，他們爲了生存而與大自然奮鬥。他們狩獵爲生，當他們没有冬糧的時候，他們必須冒險的獵取海馬或白熊之類。他們是文明世界之外的人羣，他們没有銳利的軍器，甚至於没有一枚鐵針。他們之間没有戰爭或任何仇怨。他們和平而仁愛的生活着，他們不懂得文明人一切奸詐虚僞的行爲。

然而正因爲如此，他們被帝國主義的白種人當作無知識的野蠻人。於是白種人便以幾盒鐵針或一根鳥槍以換取他們無數極珍貴的獸皮，而且任意淫狎他們的婦女。然而他們可以禮讓的從他人的妻女身上得着安慰，却不能任自己的妻女給文明人强暴的奸汚，所以他們反抗着，殺死了人面獸心的所謂文明人。他們不懂得法律，他們也不知道什麽是他們應受的刑罰。當馬拉被文明人欺騙的擒獲之後，他才知道自己新手救活的白種人，現在是將自己置於死地的劊子手了。他們爲了自由與和平，到底挣脫了帝國主義的枷鎖。他們從白種那裏所受到的毒害是在雪地冰天中逃走。他們不會使用文明人之軍器以獵取野獸，在飢餓中只好殺家大充飢。

啊！在這裏暴露了文明人的奸詐，虚僞，殘暴，乃至於一切帝國主義的眞面目。被認爲野蠻民族的「愛斯基摩」的人們，除了與大自然努力奮鬥之外，還得逃避所謂文明人的毒害。在這裏使我們立刻想起了布朶敷金的「亞洲風雲」。原始生活的蒙古人，被帝國主義者欺騙虐待，壓迫，乃至於慘無人道的屠殺，到最後原始的蒙古人到底起來了，到底揭穿了帝國主義的眞面目而發動了反帝戰爭。同樣，在這「愛斯基摩」的作者却没有更進一步的認識，范達克所能做到的只有以眞實的同情來描寫這原始的人羣之可愛的生活和個性。他祗知道他們應當爲愛情而反抗，他只對於帝國主義者加以側面的譏諷，他熱忱的同情野蠻人之運命，直至馬拉被驅逐於溶解了的冰塊上逃亡時，他使那年輕的白種人發現天良的而不將他置於死地。

如上所述，我們當然不能在美國發現與布朶敷金一樣的導演，然而有了這一影片，也未嘗不是美國影片中之珍貴的寳物。我們看罷，在對白中他咒駡了所謂文明人，他坦白的敎純樸的「愛斯基摩」的人們仇恨英國人而與文明人斷絶往來。其同情被壓迫民族與憤恨帝國主義的熱情，充分的流露於畫面之間。

不錯，他是一個進步的人道主義者，他有着自由主義的世界觀。在這影片中，雖然是傷感也罷，他究竟是偉大的展開了被壓迫民族之痛苦。誰是野蠻人？請大家想想罷。

重說一句，在没有進一步的理解之前，他所能做到的只是人道主義的傷感。當他在最後用首極沉痛的葛雷菲士在「賴婚」中所用的手法的時候，他使馬拉在雪地中逃亡。没有食物在殺盡了家狗之後，再與野狼搏鬥。爲了逃避白人之絞刑，只得在溶解着冰塊上帶着妻子隨波逐流，乃至於不知所終。這悲哀沉痛的詩的情調，無疑的深深地刺激了觀衆的心胸。所以，在導演手法上，其最成功的便是調子上的捉摸。至於畫面的整潔，對於每一愛情塲面之細膩，以及對於狩獵塲面之緊張，可謂神妙之至。難道還有誰認爲母親喂乳或馬拉之後妻的袒胸歌唱是誨淫的「香艶」「肉感」嗎？他於地地的風聲，寒夜之犬的哀鳴，……其善於處理聲片之音響，於此可見。至於幾個「愛斯基摩」藉的演員，如男主角飾馬拉者云兩個女主角，都演得極好，特别是男主角在挣脫鐵練時，與飾其後妻者在小屋中歌唱時；更顯出表演的天才。據說這二人已爲范達克先生帶回好萊塢了。

總之，這是一部極有價値的影片。謹介紹於讀者諸君之前。

評「地獄英雌」 138

— 羅平

BloodMoney丨南京丨

「博愛里」是粗獷的，生動的，有一種奔放的氣勢，雖然它是意識地宣傳着帝國主義的侵略戰爭，但我們可以從那裏看到美國下層社會的眞實。

而「地獄英雌」却是幽雅的，平凡的，用紆緩的調子描寫了一個戀愛故事，然而所謂下層生活的暴露，除了開頭有一些夜總會裏的草裙艶舞，靡靡之音以外，簡直看不到什麽了。

但是，我們得承認，美國的確有着像培萊這樣的下層社會的巨霸。

他是一個結交官府，專以債劵代人具保的流氓。他的生活是玩女人，玩跑狗塲，打高而夫球，完全是個遊手好閒之徒。

另一種的人物是特魯意，專做巨案的大盜，然而我們不能從他的外表看出來。

我們不能從培萊與持魯意的身上找出根本不同的社會背景，他們都是近代都市中流氓無産者的上層分子。因之，我們從「地獄英雌」中只能看到他們的文雅的享樂的生活，而不是粗率的遊蕩生活。

然而，「地獄英雌」中的愛蘭玲却是更値得我們注意的。

美國資本主義的發展已達到爛熟　，一切的社會的上升與進步，都已停止，而只能看出它的衰减，死亡，腐朽的徵候，雖然我們特别應該指出那裏生長着的一種新興的朝氣的因素

近代社會的權勢者的生活，因之達到了一個墮落的，平凡的，醜惡的最高點，於是一切的最大的需要是不平凡的剌激，在那没有了絲毫生氣的社會羣中流行着空想與好奇。

女子在近代社會的解放，本來是不澈底的，然而現在，畸形的社會制度下的女子已不能滿足，性的享樂，以及其他一切高級的雅緻的享樂生活，於是她們更發展了好奇與空想。在美國，女子選擇丈夫的標凖，竟有捨棄紳士，而就流氓者，無非是這種現象的一種精華。

愛蘭玲便是這樣的女子，從這裏，我們却可以看出美國社會的腐朽的程度，和新因素的成長與揚棄這個舊社會的必然丨雖然「地獄英雌」的劇作者是不會理解到這一點的。

演員中的喬治貝洛夫，他在一年前不高興攝製他不願演的影片而脫離了「電影圈」，現在重進了二十世紀公司，因爲他的願意，我們在銀幕上看到的，也覺得他確很努力。

導演的手法用「劃過」甚多，而他的零亂，總有點不可掩飾的被我們感覺着。

電影小說

凱塞琳女皇SearletEmpress 139

— 素梅

亞萊克賽於是就獻上禮物，送給蘇斐亞的係到北方去用的禦寒之物，送給育漢娜的是俄國女皇的一幀御容，四面鑲嵌着珍寳。育漢娜一方面向大使道謝，一方面因旣蘇斐亞默然無言，覺得有些生氣，就示意給她，呌她說話。蘇斐亞粉面上起了一陣紅雲，好看着俄國女皇的御容，就問亞萊賽道：「你没有帶一個皇太子的像來嗎？」亞萊克賽公爵笑道：「你要呌他比一切的男子還要好看嗎？」蘇斐亞露着侷促的神氣道：「可不是嗎。」亞萊克賽道：「好，皇太子正是你所希望的，或者還要好些。他有高高的身材，像一個希臘的神。他的眼睛，像青天般青，他的頭髮，像烏木那樣光緻。他的强壯，可以敵得住一隊牛。他現在廢寢忘食的等待你去。」公爵話雖滔滔不絶地說着，但是他的眼睛，好像罩了一層黑紗，隱藏着什麽秘密似的。蘇斐亞的母親吩咐她退出去，她就很客氣地向亞萊克賽道了謝，退出去了。她到門口的時候，她又躊躇了下下，回過頭來向那遠道來的大使瞟了一眼。她的心跳躍着，就像驚鴻似的，飛奔上樓到自己的寢室裏去了。她到了寢室裏，就把她的洋囡囡取了出來。她和它低低地說道：「蘇斐亞弗勒德里加，你開心嗎？你要嫁人了你要有男人了。我就是你的俄國丈夫，一個大大的俄國大公皇太子。我們不久就要結婚了。」她說完了，默然地深思着。她立卽覺得好像有什麽畏懼似的，使她的雙眉緊縐起來。她將離開自己的家庭，……離開她親愛的父親，……離開她的母親，她在婚禮告成之後，當然要回到普魯士的，……她的保姆卡都爾，……她的敎授華格臬，……以及他所知道習慣的一切生活，……去到那遠在北方，生疏，寒冷的異域，……她又想到那俄國大使送來的皮衣和暖水袋等，她就覺得有些不寒而慄了。（未完）

The Central Political Council Approves 24 Members of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee, including Yunduan Wangchuk

Special Appointments of He Yingqin and Zhao Daiwen as Chief and Deputy Chief Instructors 2

The Organizational Regulations of the Mongolian Autonomous Political Affairs Committee are Promulgated

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council held its 398th meeting on the morning of the 7th. Over 30 people attended, including Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Ju Zheng, Gu Mengyu, Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Gongbo, Shao Yuanchong, Kong Xiangxi, Bai Yunti, and Ke Xing'e. Wang Zhaoming chaired the meeting and resolved: (1) To specially appoint He Yingqin as the Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia and Zhao Daiwen as the Deputy Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia. To appoint 24 people, including Yunduan Wangchuk, Suonamu Labutan, Shakdorjab, Enke Batu, Bai Yunti, and Ke Xing'e, as members of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee, designating Yunduan Wangchuk as Chairman and Suonamu Labutan and Shakdorjab as Vice Chairmen; (2) To retroactively recognize the National Government's explicit appointment of Li Jun as the Minister to Peru; (3) To retroactively recognize the National Government's explicit special appointment of Gu Weijun as the special envoy to attend the funeral of the former King of Belgium and the coronation ceremony of the new King, with Zhang Naiyan as the deputy envoy. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) It is reported that the Central Government decided on the 7th that He Yingqin and Zhao Daiwen will serve as the senior officials sent to Mongolia to guide autonomy. If He and Zhao cannot go due to circumstances, they may send representatives to go. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) The organizational regulations of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee have been passed, with 24 members. The organization is divided into two departments and four sections, and a finance committee. The expenses requested by the Mongolian representatives, etc., were 50,000 yuan per month. President Wang indicated that it is hoped that it can be allocated accordingly. As for the candidates for senior officials to guide Inner Mongolian autonomy, He Yingqin is internally decided. It is heard that He's consent is still required. The representatives of the various leagues and banners will return north within this week due to the passage of the organizational regulations, leaving one or two representatives in Nanjing to negotiate everything. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

Full Text of the Provisional Organization Outline 3

(Nanjing) Provisional Organization Outline of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee: Article 1: The Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee is organized in accordance with the principles of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Measures promulgated by the National Government. Article 2: This committee is directly under the Executive Yuan and is under the guidance of the central competent authorities and the central guiding officials to handle local autonomous political affairs in various leagues and banners. In the event of incidents involving provinces, it shall consult with the provincial governments to handle them. Article 3: The address of this committee shall be located in Beile Temple. Article 4: This committee shall have 9 to 24 members, who shall be appointed by the National Government upon submission by the Executive Yuan, and one chairman and two vice chairmen shall be designated from among the members. Article 5: This committee shall hold a meeting every two weeks. When necessary, special meetings may be convened. In the previous meeting, the chairman shall be the chairman. When a member is unable to attend due to circumstances, a representative may be sent to attend. Article 6: The chairman of this committee shall execute the resolutions of the meeting in the preceding article, handle the meeting, and supervise the subordinates and agencies. The vice-chairman shall assist the chairman in handling the affairs of the committee. When the chairman is unable to perform his duties, one of the vice-chairmen shall act on his behalf. Article 7: This committee shall have the following departments in charge, which shall respectively handle all the affairs of the committee: the Secretariat shall handle matters such as documents, records, statistics, translation, accounting, and general affairs; the Counselor's Office shall draft and review the committee's plans, laws, bills, and orders; the Department of Civil Affairs shall handle matters related to civil affairs; the Security Department shall handle matters related to security; the Industry Department shall handle matters related to industry; the Education Department shall handle matters related to education; and the Finance Committee shall handle matters related to finance. The above departments shall be divided into sections to handle affairs, except for the Counselor's Office. All departments should consider the circumstances and submit separate requests for establishment, except for the Secretariat and Counselor's Office. Article 8: This committee shall have the following staff in each department: Secretary-General of the Secretariat, one person, a senior appointment; four secretaries with delegated authority; one director of the Counselor's Office, a senior appointment; four counselors with delegated authority; honorary councilors with recommended authority, one person elected by each of the former banners, with a term of one year, which may be renewed; one director of each department, a senior appointment; one chairman of the Finance Committee, a senior appointment; six to ten members, who shall be concurrently appointed by the chairman from among the secretaries, counselors, and councilors; the directors of each department shall be ex officio members; twelve to sixteen section chiefs in all departments, with recommended authority; forty to sixty staff members in all departments, appointed by the committee. This committee may employ various technical personnel and employees at its discretion. Article 9: The appointment of Mongolians as members of this committee shall be the principle. The staff of all departments under this committee shall be selected by the Executive Yuan from within the country who are familiar with the situation in Mongolia and have specialized knowledge. Article 10: The meeting rules and office rules of this committee shall be determined by this committee and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. Article 11: This outline shall be implemented upon promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

Regulations for the Office of the Chief Instructor 4

(Nanjing) Provisional Regulations of the Office of the Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia: Article 1: The Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia, under the order of the Executive Yuan and according to the principles of the Mongolian Local Autonomy Measures promulgated by the National Government, shall guide the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee and mediate disputes between provinces and counties and leagues and banners. Article 2: There shall be one Chief Instructor and one Deputy Chief Instructor, who shall be specially appointed by the National Government upon submission by the Executive Yuan. Article 3: The Office of the Chief Instructor shall have two consultants, who shall be appointed by the Executive Yuan upon submission by the Chief Instructor. Article 4: Other staff of the Office of the Chief Instructor shall be determined separately. Article 5: When the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee holds a meeting, the Chief Instructor and Deputy Chief Instructor may send consultants to attend and provide guidance. Article 6: All official documents of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee submitted to the Executive Yuan and the Mongolian Tibetan Affairs Commission shall be submitted to the Office of the Chief Instructor at the same time. Article 7: If the Chief Instructor deems it inappropriate to handle incidents and issue orders by the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee, he may correct and revoke them. Article 8: The expenses of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee shall be transferred by the Office of the Chief Instructor. Article 9: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

Order of the National Government 5

(Nanjing) The National Government ordered on the 7th: Now that the Provisional Organizational Outline of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee has been formulated, it is hereby promulgated. This is the order. Also ordered: Now that the Provisional Regulations of the Office of the Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia have been formulated, they are hereby promulgated. This is the order. Also ordered: He Yingqin is specially appointed as the Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia, and Zhao Daiwen is the Deputy Chief Instructor for Local Autonomy in Mongolia. This is the order. Also ordered: Yunduan Wangchuk, Suonamu Labutan, Shakdorjab, Demchugdongrub, Alatan Ochir, Babaodorji, Hao Yantu, Yangsang Enke Batu, Bai Yunti, Ke Xing'e, Wu Heling, Chotebazarap, Gungchuk Rashida, Li Zayatu, Bhibayarongxiang, Nyima Otsoel, Yideqin Guoerzuerzabu, Toktohupan Di Gongchabu, Namlo Lese Lengayule, and Wu Gui are appointed as members of the Mongolian Local Autonomous Political Affairs Committee, and Yunduan Wangchuk is designated as the Chairman, and Suonamu Labutan and Shakdorjab are the Vice Chairmen. This is the order. (Central Telegram of the 7th)

Mongolian Representatives Will Soon Leave Nanjing 6

(Nanjing) Guoer Zhuoerzabu, the representative of De Wang, stated that the Mongolian autonomy issue has been resolved by the Central Government. On the afternoon of the 7th, he visited the ministers of various ministries to bid farewell. He plans to travel to Ping with the Mongolian representatives to Nanjing the day after tomorrow and return to Mongolia. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) Zhao Taibao and other representatives of various Mongolian leagues, with their mission completed, will discuss again on the 8th and return north to Mongolia on the 9th to report on their mission. The Autonomous Political Affairs Committee will begin organizing once the representatives arrive. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

The Kang and Tibetan Armies are in a Stalemate in Guanyin Temple 7

(Nanjing) A representative of the people of Xikang said that the Kang and Tibetan armies are currently in a stalemate in Guanyin Temple. Dengkebu was once lost but was retaken by the Kang army. The current situation is still unknown. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) Gongjue Zhongni, the Tibetan representative in Nanjing, told someone that the conflict between Kang and Tibet was only seen in the newspapers. This office has not received any telegrams from the Tibetan government. The current ruling authorities in Tibet are very enthusiastic in supporting the Central Government. According to my speculation, those currently in conflict with the Kang army are definitely not formal Tibetan troops, or they are lamas from the Da Jie Temple, retaliating against me. Because the truth is unknown, I have sent a telegram to inquire, and a reply should arrive in Nanjing in ten days. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

Panchen's Representative, An Qin, Returns from Eastern Tibet 8

(Nanjing) Panchen sent representative An Qin to Tibet last year to discuss Tibetan affairs with the Dalai Lama. After the Dalai Lama passed away, he also represented Panchen in paying tribute. Now that An has completed his work in Tibet, he has returned from Tibet via India and will arrive in Nanjing next month. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) Yu Chan donated 100 horses to the military academy. The school has now sent personnel to Zhangjiakou to collect them and transport them to Nanjing. In addition, a large number of warhorses seized from the rebels have also been transported from Fujian to the school. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

Meng Shiquan's brigade of Lu Dachang's troops has advanced towards Ningxia [illegible], Lu is still staying in the province. Lu Fengnian, the division commander of Sun's troops, and Sun Ziyu, Dou Lianxi, Xie Putian, and Peng Zhenguo, the brigade commanders, telegraphed Zhu Shaoliang and Deng Baoshan, deciding to lead their troops to station in Pingluo Dengkou Shizuizi to await reorganization, requesting friendly forces not to attack them. A meeting between Fu and Sun can be arranged, but there is no guarantee that Sun can be persuaded to leave the army. Therefore, the authorities are still actively proceeding with military operations according to the planned steps. If Sun is still not aware, there is only a way to implement the encirclement and suppression. The fighting in Ningyuan has only had minor contact in recent days. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) After Fu Zuoyi arrived in Baotou, he telegraphed He yesterday, reporting that his troops are continuously advancing westward from Linhe to Dengkou. He will go to Linhe to inspect Zhao Chengshou's troops. There has been no telegram from Fu Zhan Kui and Li Ming after they advanced westward. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

The Central Political Council Studies the Puppet Usurping the Throne Incident 10

The Consistent Attitude Will Not Change

(Nanjing) Regarding the incident of the puppet Puyi usurping the throne and claiming to be emperor, how should China respond? The Legislative Yuan suggested to the Central Political Conference. It is heard that the Central Political Conference today had a detailed study of this and has generally adopted it. It is generally believed that the responsibility for the Northeast Three Provinces and the Rehe problem has its own reasons. China will never change its consistent attitude. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

The Southwest Region Sends a Circular Telegram Condemning Puyi's Usurpation of the Throne 11

(Hong Kong) The Executive Committee of the Political Council sent a circular telegram on the 6th condemning Puyi's usurpation of the throne. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) The National Diplomatic Association held a meeting to discuss the issue of condemning the puppet's usurpation of the throne. Tian Jiongjin, Yu Nengmo, and Ma Hetian were appointed to form a committee to study it together, and Huang Youchang was appointed to draft a declaration. The content is: (1) Please ask all countries in the world to pay attention to the actions of the puppet Manchukuo and unanimously deny it; (2) Call on the people of the whole country to rise up and condemn it; (3) Ask the government to find ways to punish the activities of traitors. The declaration will be published soon. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

The Japanese and Puppets at Gubeikou Have Not Yet Withdrawn 12

The Puppet Agencies Have Also Not Moved Out of the Pass

(Beiping) After the administrative section of Gubeikou was taken over, the Jimi District Office, Zuo Zhi Bureau, and Public Security Bureau established by our side were also established at the same time. The puppet state's agencies in Gubei only moved the addresses of the houses to the northeast and west of the Chaohe River and did not withdraw outside the pass. The 25th Regiment of the Japanese Army, Yongjian, is still stationed in the town. According to people from Gubeikou, the puppet state border police team at Nantianmen has not withdrawn. There are still four puppet police officers on the north side of Nantianmen, one Chinese, one Japanese, and two Koreans, checking travelers' cars for half an hour, which proves that the puppet police have not withdrawn. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Tianjin) The provincial government allocated 6,000 yuan, and the Miyun county magistrate repaired 190 miles of long-distance telephone lines in the Gubeikou Gaoliying section. The Gaoli-Miyun section will continue to raise funds for repairs. (Telegram of the 7th)

(Tianjin) The Hebei postal bureau has begun to accept and send mail to Gubeikou, and the local post office has been restored. On the 7th, Yin Rugeng told someone that the matter of the Japanese army occupying our houses and withdrawing outside Gubeikou has been handed over to the Gubeikou Office of the Jimo Administrative Commissioner's Office to handle on the spot and does not require him to go again. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

Chiang Issues a Proclamation to the People on Handling Recovered Bandit Area Land 13

(Nanchang) Chiang issued a proclamation to the people on handling recovered bandit area land, explaining in a question-and-answer format the allocation of land based on population and the reorganization of all land to achieve the goal of tillers owning their land. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanchang) Chiang said about the land recovered from the bandit areas: (1) To return all the land to the original owners to determine ownership, and to allocate land based on population to achieve the goal of tillers owning their land. Establish rural restoration committees at all levels to clear up business rights and ensure that farmers have land to cultivate. (2) To generally organize and use cooperatives to lend capital to farmers. (3) Rent arrears owed by tenants during the bandit occupation are not allowed to be recovered, and even old debts can only be cleared up slowly to reassure people. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

Japanese Commander Nakamura Bids Farewell to Yu Xuezhong 14

(Tianjin) Lieutenant General Nakamura, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, went to the provincial government this afternoon to bid farewell to Yu Xuezhong. Nakamura is scheduled to return to his country on the 20th. Major General Umezu, the successor commander, will arrive in Tianjin on the 19th to take office. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) After Nakamura, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, was transferred to the commander of the 6th Division of the Japanese Army, his successor commander, Major General Umezu, has arrived in Tianjin. Nakamura has completed the handover and is scheduled to return to his country by ship tomorrow. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) Lieutenant General Ida, the former commander of the Lushun Fortress and the current director of the 3rd Department of the Japanese Ministry of the Army, was dispatched by the authorities of the Ministry to inspect the recent deployment of the Japanese garrison in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe, and is scheduled to visit Beiping on the 13th to visit the military and political authorities. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) Nakamura, the former commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, has been transferred to the commander of the 6th Division and is scheduled to take a ship back to his country on the 8th. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

The Formal Note is Delivered to the Embassy

It is learned that the External Affairs Department, based on the request in the reply, once again sent a note to the US government, presenting key points for ordering a new commercial treaty. This note has been formally delivered to the US Embassy. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

The Yutian Security Team Decides to Thoroughly Reorganize 16

Yin Rugeng and Han Dianbang Meet Yu to Negotiate

And Summon the Yutian County Magistrate to Discuss Together

(Beiping) Regarding the post-disaster reorganization and disbandment of the Yutian Special Police, Yin Rugeng and Han Dianbang, the internally appointed captain of the Hebei Provincial Government Special Police Brigade, went to Tianjin yesterday to meet Yu to discuss it. It is currently being discussed and will be decided soon. Captain Han's order can also be officially announced. Yin and Jia Degan meet with our diplomatic authorities for their first conversation after taking office

(Nanjing) Jia Degan went to the External Affairs Department at 3:00 PM on the 7th to meet with our diplomatic authorities for his first diplomatic conversation. It is heard that a preliminary exchange of views was made on the matter of British merchants invading Yunnan to mine. He did not leave until 4:30 PM. Regarding the issue of revising the Sino-British commercial treaty, the British government has not yet replied, and Ambassador Jia has not yet received instructions from the government. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

(Nanjing) The Sino-British Cultural Association and the Nanjing Returned British Students Association hosted a banquet for Jia Degan at the Lizhi Society on the 7th. Jia, Wang Shijie, Zhang Daofan, Zheng Tianxi, Ying Geling, and Taike Man attended. At the banquet, President Wang Shijie gave a speech first, stating that due to the close friendly relations between China and Britain, it is an important element in promoting relations between Eastern and Western countries in industry, commerce, and culture. Sir Jia has a grand vision for his mission and new prospects. It is firmly believed that his rich experience will not only achieve significant results in official work, but also make great contributions to promoting Sino-British cultural relations in a broader and more meaningful way. He sincerely hopes that Sir Jia will give support and close cooperation in the position of comrade. Then Jia replied, saying that he was very pleased with the establishment of the Cultural Association and hoped that all parties would do their best for the cause of the Association, so as not to fail Ambassador Lan Qian and President Wang's wishes. (Nanjing) The British Ambassador is scheduled to visit the Panchen Lama on the morning of the 8th to discuss Tibetan affairs, and will go to Hubei on the 10th to inspect British expatriates, staying for two or three days before returning to Nanjing and heading north. (Beiping) Yin Rugeng will return to Beiping on the 2nd and go to Yutian again to carry out the handling. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng went to Tianjin yesterday to meet Yu to report on the process of taking over Gubeikou and asked for instructions on how to deal with the Yutian county magistrate. He Xiaoyi, the head of the office in Beiping, went to Tianjin that evening to assist Yin in handling everything. According to relevant sources, in addition to the two small ports near Gubeikou that have been taken over, the three small ports such as Baimaguan Daxiaoyu Shitou Road have not been taken over because there are still more than 100 Japanese puppet troops who have not withdrawn. Negotiations will be held with the Japanese side, and the Japanese Embassy will send a telegram to the Kwantung Army. The Embassy has received a reply telegram, saying that after Matsui returns to Changchun, the Japanese troops in the three ports will be ordered to withdraw. However, due to the authority of the puppet army, the Japanese side can only notify the puppet military authorities to order the withdrawal. Therefore, the withdrawal date of the puppet army will inevitably be slower. Jie Tian The shortest time can be realized. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Tianjin) At noon on the 7th, Yin Rugeng and Han Zexin, the newly appointed captain of the Yutian Security Brigade, went to the provincial government to ask Yu Xuezhong for his opinion on the reorganization of the Yutian garrison. They will go to Yutian in two or three days to implement the reorganization. The number of people is determined to be 1,000. 800 people who were recruited at will by the unit during the rebellion period will be given dismissal pay and sent away. After the reorganization is completed, they will be transferred to another place to garrison. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

Routine Meeting of the Beiping Military Branch 18

(Beiping) The routine meeting of the Military Branch this morning resolved to restrict the issuance of special expenses to various troops, publicly elected Ji Yiqiao as a standing member of the Military Training Council, and decided to temporarily suspend the work of the Procurement Committee. (Special Dispatch of the 7th)

(Beiping) The 47th Standing Committee meeting of the Military Branch was held on the morning of the 7th. More than 20 people attended, including Rong Zhen, Jiang Bocheng, Shang Zhen, Ji Yiqiao, Zou Zuohua, Men Zhizhong, Bao Wenyue, Wei Zonghan, and Wei Yisan. The meeting was chaired by He Yingqin and resolved: (1) Publicly elected Ji Yiqiao as a standing member of the Military Training Committee of this branch; (2) The procurement committee of this branch will be temporarily suspended. In the future, the procurement of equipment, machinery, and military supplies will be the responsibility of each division, but it must be approved by the management and supervision committee in advance and submitted for acceptance after the event; (2) A temporary motion stated that the Military Branch was in financial difficulty. In the future, if various troops request special expenses beyond the budget, if they cannot be paid out of temporary expenses, they cannot be issued until funds are available. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. (Central News Agency dispatch of the 7th)

Current Commentary

Quickly Eliminate the Harm of Red Pills and White Powder 21

Our country's biggest harm in the north recently is not necessarily from imperialists, nor necessarily from bandits and local bullies and corrupt officials, but from the general decline of life that comes from the decline of the rural economy, followed by the harm of red pills and white powder. Based on the general situation, observing society, we cannot find the benefits of red pills and white powder anywhere. Even those who take red pills and white powder believe it is very harmful. Then why must they take it? Why do they knowingly choose this chronic suicidal policy?

I believe the biggest reason is the abnormal phenomenon of the rural economy being on the verge of bankruptcy. Farmers' lives in the provinces and regions north of the Yellow River are even more difficult. Even in years of good harvest, ordinary farmers cannot exchange their labor for their minimum necessary living needs. Therefore, two phenomena are found in northern rural areas: one is that the nutrition of farmers' lives is insufficient, and their physical strength gradually declines with insufficient nutrition. Although northern farmers are said to have relatively strong inherited bones and thicker qualities, most ordinary farmers now have hungry faces, showing signs of insufficient nutrition. Thus, work efficiency naturally declines. However, in terms of social needs, they are required to dedicate all their abilities, so they naturally seek a stimulant that is sufficient to excite them. Another is that the northern rural economy has evolved into a lifeless state. Ordinary people cannot even support their necessary lives, and all other entertainment is naturally completely absent. However, ordinary people always need entertainment. Since proper and beneficial entertainment is not available, they can only seek momentary stimulation, treating this stimulation as happiness. Moreover, taking red pills and white powder is more convenient than smoking opium, so it has spread universally.

This situation was limited to a small number of people and a small number of regions in the past few years. Although the harm was very severe, it was not very great. If we could do our best to ban it and impose legal sanctions, it would not be difficult to eliminate it. However, now this kind of poison is spread very widely in the northern provinces and regions. Even ordinary urban workers have a lot of infections. Recently, it has also spread from north to south, and the lower-class masses in the Yangtze River basin are also suffering from infection. Unexpectedly, the harm of red pills and white powder has become a major problem for the entire China.

We can still awaken the masses to fight for national interests against imperialist aggression. Bandits and local bullies and corrupt officials can be eradicated as long as we can seriously rectify politics. Only the poison of red pills and white powder, once addicted, becomes more and more toxic. A good person becomes a useless person, and a group of good people also becomes a group of useless people. Because ordinary people always need a healthy physique to bear heavy burdens and carry out major events. If the physique is bad, both big and small things will be impossible to carry out. Moreover, this kind of harm is inherited, not only is the current economy in trouble, but the future may inevitably lead to bankruptcy, and even make future generations suffer the same pain. This is seriously related to the rise and fall of the race and the survival of the nation, so we must not take this matter lightly.

From a passive point of view, persuading people to quit and strictly prohibiting its sale is the only urgent measure. But we have all tried or are vigorously promoting it, and what is its effectiveness? We can fully understand this by looking at the situation in Shanxi. In other words, in the current situation of global recession, it is unlikely that people will not do wrong, that people will abide by the law and know shame, and that people will not try to make windfall profits. Therefore, in addition to imposing sanctions from a passive point of view, we should also supplement it with active measures.

We believe that active measures should not only prohibit the sale of poisons, but also fundamentally prevent people from taking them. Naturally, the method of preventing people from taking them is not easy, nor can it be effective in a short period of time. Because the force of social sanctions [i.e., public morality, public right and wrong criticism] cannot be cultivated in a short period of time. The cultivation of education and the cultivation of knowledge both require a considerable amount of time. What is particularly important is the stability of the economic foundation. If we can improve the living standards of ordinary people in rural areas, rebuild the rural economy that is on the verge of decline, and farmers know that they can live and develop upwards, and then promote public, proper, and rational entertainment, then this kind of poison that only has a temporary stimulating effect will naturally disappear.

Japan Still Seeks to Salvage Cotton Industry Negotiations with Britain 24

(London) - After 30 minutes of negotiations between Britain and Japan, they were changed to private discussions, and then the meeting was resumed, but no agreement could be reached, and the meeting was adjourned immediately. A statement was later released, stating that the conference had reached a dead end on the issue of the scope of discussion. This is regrettable for both British and Japanese representatives. However, in view of the seriousness of this issue, it was agreed to postpone the meeting until tomorrow.

(7th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) - The failure of the British-Japanese cotton textile industry negotiations has now been confirmed. However, both sides want to shift the responsibility for the failure to the other side, so the representatives of the two countries may not openly announce a break at today's meeting. The current question is whether the British government will immediately take retaliatory measures after the failure of the negotiations. According to general opinion,

If the British Empire completely prohibits the import of Japanese goods, domestic prices will inevitably rise, which is not what the British government wants. Therefore, a complete ban on the import of Japanese goods will be difficult to achieve. The British government will try to contact Western countries that are also affected by Japanese competition, so as to unite with each other for protection. Regarding this matter, it is heard that Britain has already started negotiations with the Netherlands. (7th Havas Dispatch)

(London) - This morning's meeting of representatives of the British and Japanese organizing industries did indeed come to a standstill. However, because the matter is important, the meeting was postponed until tomorrow. It is heard that this postponement was the result of contact between the Lancashire representatives and the British government. This deadlock was caused by the question of whether the scope of discussion should include the world market or only the British and its colonial markets. If the negotiations completely break down, the demands for protecting the British business market and preventing Japanese competition will inevitably become more intense than before, and this issue may be handled by diplomatic means. (7th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) - The atmosphere of the meeting between the British and Japanese people's representatives on the 7th was quite dangerous. The Japanese representatives had a strong attitude and did not hesitate to break up the meeting. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, hoping that the meeting would be successful, has ordered Ambassador Matsudaira in Britain to contact the Japanese delegation to prepare to resolve the crisis. According to Japanese observations, the result of the breakdown of the British-Japanese meeting is that the Manchester cotton industry in Britain will inevitably advocate (1) abolishing the British-Japanese Treaty of Commerce, (2) excluding all Japanese-made goods, and (3) third countries with economic relations with Britain should unanimously join the front line and implement the anti-Japanese goods movement. The British government, which had previously appeased the anti-Japanese movement, will also resort to extraordinary measures. The Japanese government feels that the occurrence of this kind of incident is unfortunate, and intends to resolve the negotiations by the governments of the two countries. Preparations are now underway. The post-mortem negotiations between Ambassador Matsudaira and British businessman Francis are likely to be realized soon. (7th Japan United Electric)

(London) - The representatives of the Lancashire side attending the British-Japanese meeting arrived in London late on the 6th, and said that if the Japanese side's attitude does not change drastically at the final stage, the main meeting on the 7th will inevitably break down. It is also heard that when this inevitable situation arises, the Lancashire representatives and others have already made detailed studies on future countermeasures. Their opinions are roughly as follows: The breakdown of the British-Japanese meeting is very regrettable, but even if it breaks down, the position of the British cotton industry will still be solid, because the total amount of British imports accounts for 15% of the world, and its exports only account for 6%. Moreover, if Britain concludes this kind of trade agreement with various countries in the future, it will be extremely beneficial compared to Japan. Therefore, if the meeting on the 7th ends in a breakdown, Britain and its directly governed colonies should adopt a double import discount system to protect them. (7th Japan United Electric)

(Tokyo) - The British-Japanese cotton industry meeting is facing an impasse due to opposing opinions and cannot be salvaged. It is feared that the meeting today will break down immediately. The Japanese foreign affairs authorities are studying the policies to be adopted in the future. The foreign affairs authorities believe that if the British-Japanese meeting breaks down, it is necessary to leave room for the possibility of continuing negotiations in the future. Ambassador Matsudaira to Britain is also making every effort in this regard. However, before the start of the meeting, the British side had petitioned the British government that if the meeting breaks down one day, please raise tariffs on Japanese goods and abolish the British-Japanese Treaty of Commerce. In view of this, the Japanese government believes that if the negotiations break down, the British government will definitely consider what measures to take. If the British government intends to transfer the issue to government negotiations, the Japanese side also intends to agree. At this time, it will not be limited to cotton industry relations, but will take a broader view of the overall situation of British-Japanese trade and draft specific proposals to adjust the entirety of British-Japanese trade and engage in negotiations. (7th Dentsu Dispatch)

Dutch East Indies Resists Japanese Goods, Japanese Chamber of Commerce Protests

(Tokyo) - Because the Dutch East Indies government will restrict the import of Japanese goods, the Japan Chamber of Commerce and Industry has adopted strict measures, and will suggest that all national chambers of commerce and industry approve it, hoping to promote diplomatic negotiations by the Japanese government authorities. Today, the following recommendations have been submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry: The Dutch East Indies has previously restricted the import of cement, beer, and salong. This time, it has implemented an unfair distribution system for bleached cloth, and plans to implement the same distribution system for general groceries. If so, Japan's sales routes over the past 30 years will completely collapse. At this juncture, it is hoped that the government will strongly protest to the Dutch East Indies government and seek effective and appropriate measures. (7th Dentsu Dispatch)

(Tokyo) - Today, the Tokyo Chamber of Commerce and Industry sent a telegram in the name of Chairman Go to the Governor of the Dutch East Indies, the Minister of Dutch Colonies, and the Dutch East Indies Chamber of Commerce, protesting as follows: The import distribution to be implemented by the Dutch East Indies will have an adverse impact on the trade relations between Japan and the Dutch East Indies. I hope you will be cautious. The Economic Alliance will also convene a standing committee on the 8th and then issue a protest telegram with the same purpose. (7th Dentsu Dispatch)

Japanese Suicide Rate Averages Seven Per Day 26

More than 2,000 People in Tokyo in One Year

Most Causes are Due to Economic Relations

(Tokyo) - According to authorities' investigations, the number of suicides in Japan has been gradually increasing recently. Last year, the number of suicides in Tokyo Prefecture totaled 2,551 (including 1,052 women). On average, seven men and women commit suicide every day. This is an increase of 194 people compared to the previous year's statistics. The peak period for suicides is in the spring and the lowest in the winter. The ratio of spring to winter is ten to six. The most common reasons for suicide are pessimism and illness, followed by love affairs and emotional relationships, and then by financial difficulties, mental disorder and family discord. However, most of them are mainly due to economic relations. Suicides are more common among young people who are full of gratitude. There are 498 young men and women under the age of 20 who abandon their future and choose death, and 1,146 people between the ages of 20 and 30. (7th Japan United Electric)

Colonial Minister's answer,

I have not yet known about the Kwantung Army's plan.

Bando asked,

What is the state of Chinese immigration to "Manchukuo"?

Colonial Minister's answer,

Recently, it has been about 400,000 people per year, but most of them are laborers.

Bando asked,

Are there any countermeasures for Japanese immigration to Manchuria? Is it to provide special convenience?

Colonial Minister's answer,

The governments of Japan and Manchuria are currently negotiating the situation of giving each other convenience.

Bando asked,

How will the land ownership situation of Manchurian immigrants be protected?

Colonial Minister's answer,

The governments of Japan and Manchuria are also negotiating the confirmation of land ownership for immigrants. (7th Japan United Electric)

US Senate Passes Huge Navy Bill 35

Five-Year Plan with Expenses of One Hundred Million Yuan

Building Over One Hundred Warships and Over One Thousand Airplanes

In Preparation for Dealing with the Far East Incident

(Washington) - The US Senate today passed the most advantageous naval bill of Vinson and Trammell by a vote of 65 to 18, stipulating the construction of 102 new warships and 1,184 naval aircraft, so that the US naval power meets the limits stipulated in the 1922 Washington Naval Treaty. In order to prevent abuses, the Senate has an additional clause that limits private companies building warships to a profit of 10%. It is thought that after the bill is submitted to the House, the approval of the additional clause can be guaranteed. Senator Nye of North Dakota, who has been striving to pass this bill, said that this bill is really the savior of munitions manufacturers. This bill has no special provisions, but it is estimated that naval expenses will be between $565,000,000 and $1,000,000,000 in the next seven years. The Vinson-Trammell American naval bill is actually a merger of two bills. One was proposed by Senator Vinson of Georgia, and the other was proposed by Senator Trammell of Florida. The nature of the two bills is roughly similar, and the construction of a 15,000-ton aircraft carrier to replace the old destroyers totaling 99,900 tons and submarines of 35,530 tons is really the urgent need of the United States today, so it should be voted on first. If we use the Washington Naval Treaty to constrain it, the United States is still short of one aircraft carrier, one heavy cruiser, five light cruisers, six destroyers, and thirty submarines today. This bill plans to build 1,184 new aircraft, of which 650 are already under construction. In addition, 534 others will be put out for bidding as soon as President Roosevelt approves them. According to Admiral Standley, Chief of Naval Operations, this bill can bring the US naval air force to the limit of 2,184 aircraft allowed by the treaty. It is said that the situation in the Far East is the biggest reason for the rapid establishment of the Vinson-Trammell bill. Vinson stated that because the US naval power is weak and the United States is not prepared to deal with the incident in the Far East, the power of the United States in the Far East has been greatly weakened. (7th Guomin Dispatch)

(Washington) - Congressman Vinson, chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, previously introduced a bill requesting $380,000,000 to be allocated over five years to build 102 warships, in order to expand the US naval military power to the limit permitted by the London Naval Treaty, and another $95,000,000 to add 1,184 military aircraft. The two bills were approved by the House of Representatives on January 30 of this year, and today the Senate also passed them by a vote of 65 to 18. (6th Havas Dispatch)

However, judging from today's situation, British public opinion seems to have changed, because the fact that Britain wants to test the intentions of various countries' public opinion with a new attitude is enough to prove that the degree of opposition of most people to Britain making new promises is not as great as before. American Gang of Thieves Robs Bank in Broad Daylight 41

One Policeman Wounded in Resistance

Female Employee and Cash Stolen Together

Sioux Falls. Today, six audacious bandits robbed the Security National Bank here in broad daylight. The elaborate scheme was clearly premeditated, making it an unprecedented and shocking robbery for this area. The bandits sped to the bank entrance in a car. One person remained as the driver, while the others got out and entered the bank with a leisurely attitude. Once inside, the bandits suddenly produced guns, preventing the police inside the door from making any noise. One policeman attempted to draw his gun to resist but was shot and wounded by the bandits. The remaining police were also disarmed. All the bank employees were forbidden from moving, or they would be shot. After dividing up and seizing the cash, the bandits took a female employee out the door and into the car, using her as a shield to deter pursuers from opening fire. The car sped away. Police, alerted, pursued them to about two miles outside the city. The bandits placed the female employee in front as a shield and opened fire with a machine gun to repel the pursuers. The police, fearing they would injure the female employee, did not dare to shoot. The bandits drove another two miles or so, then abandoned their car and hijacked a passing car, speeding away. The police now believe that the ringleader must be Dillinger, the notorious bandit who escaped from Lake City Prison with a black man on March 3rd. During the pursuit, a handgun was recovered, and it was identified as belonging to Dillinger's gang. Dillinger has a long record of crimes and has escaped from prison twice. The police have now notified neighboring states and are working together to apprehend him. A close associate of Dillinger was arrested a few days ago in Pierre, South Dakota. Today, his trial for murder and prison escape began in Vermillion, South Dakota. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

The Budget of the Soviet Union 43

(TASS dispatch from Moscow, February 7th) The actual income and expenditure of the Soviet Union for 1933 were as follows: income was 39.2 billion rubles, expenditure was 36 billion rubles, resulting in a surplus of 3.2 billion rubles. The budget for 1934 is 48.879 billion rubles, an increase of 24 percent compared to the actual income and expenditure of the previous year.

Income Items: The estimated income for 1934 is as follows (in thousands of rubles):

1. Income from Socio-Economic Sectors:

(1) Trade Tax 29,227,790

(2) Special Commercial Funds 6,300,000

(3) Non-Commercial Business Tax 225,000

(4) Collective Farm Agricultural Tax 300,000

(5) Profit Tax 1,521,020

(6) Subsidies for Commercial Funds of Socialized Organizations 15,800

(7) Transportation Revenue 2,921,600

Including: Railway Transport 2,633,500

Water Transport 5,200

Other Transport 4,000

Communications 278,000

(8) National Eight Percent Bonds 445,000

(9) Currency Issuance Revenue 10,000

(10) Customs Duties and Others 2,000

(11) Income Tax from Socialized Enterprises 137,000

(12) State Farm Tax 19,900

Total Income from Socialized Economy 41,125,210

2. (1) Income from the Public 3,880,000

A. Loans 3,580,000

B. Loans from Savings Banks 300,000

(2) Taxes 2,646,000

3. Other Income 1,228,176

Total Income 48,879,461

From the above table, it can be observed that the largest source of income in this year's budget is still the trade tax (over 29 billion rubles, compared to 23 billion rubles in 1933). If trade profits are included, the total income from these two items will reach 35 billion rubles this year.

Expenditure Items: The following table shows the main expenditure items in the budget (in thousands of rubles):

1. Investment in the National Economy

(1) Heavy Industry 11,360,850

(2) Light Industry 1,157,760

(3) Film Industry 79,870

(4) Timber Industry 957,530

(5) Other Industries 1,199,100

(6) State Farms 11,905,564

(7) Collective Farms 3,974,370

(8) Food Industry of the Foodstuffs Committee 636,750

(9) Domestic Trade 3,824,660

(10) Foreign Trade 96,100

丨Reuters Special Business Report, March 7丨

Exchange Rates 45

British-American Exchange: The London foreign exchange market was calm. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to US dollars was $5.075, down 0.0125 from yesterday's closing rate. There was limited fluctuation in the morning. At 2:00 PM, the price was $5.07375, down 0.0125 from the opening.

British-French Exchange: The opening rate was 77.18 francs, up 0.15 from yesterday's closing. There were no further changes. At 2:00 PM, the price was 77.15 francs.

British-American Exchange Rate: At 2:00 PM today, the London exchange rate for New York was one British gold pound equals $5.07375, and one US dollar equals three shillings, eleven pence, 302.

American-British Exchange Rate: The closing rate for New York to British exchange yesterday was 5.07625. Today's opening was 5.0725, second session 5.0700, third session 5.0700, fourth session 5.07625, fifth session 5.07625.

Gold and Silver 46

London Gold Price: Today's London gold price was 136 shillings and 10 pence, down 4 pence from yesterday.

London Silver Bars: Today's London silver bar price was 20.375 pence for spot and 20.4375 pence for futures, both down 0.1885. The decline in silver prices is mostly due to sales from the East, with few buyers.

New York Silver Price: Today's silver market was calm, slightly looser than before, due to declines in London and Shanghai. However, the volume of sales was not large. The market situation showed signs of uncertainty. Merchants are waiting for developments. However, sentiment remains stable, expressing sympathy for the cotton and securities markets. Therefore, the opening for forward contracts was down 0.25 to 0.40 pounds from yesterday's close.

Bombay Silver Price: Today's Bombay silver market closed quietly. The spot price was 55 rupees and 10 annas, down 3 annas from yesterday.

Cotton and Wheat 47

New York Cotton: Today's opening saw limited trading, gradually stabilizing later due to good news from Liverpool and purchases from New York bankers and Liverpool.

Bombay Cotton: Today's cotton market initially fell due to long covering and futures sales, then rose due to short covering and purchases by European exporters. The price for April/May White Broach cotton was 200 rupees 75, down 1 rupee 25 from yesterday.

Liverpool Cotton: The May futures price was 6.27, down 0.03 pounds from yesterday.

Liverpool Wheat: This morning, the market situation was slightly looser. The May futures price was 4 shillings, 4 pence, 625, down 0.25.

Rubber 48

London: This afternoon, the rubber market price was firm due to rumors that American producers would participate in negotiations to limit production. The trading price for April/June was 3 pence, 1875, up 0.0625 from yesterday's price.

New York: Today's market situation was firm. Sentiment was bullish at the opening due to firm news from London and optimistic rumors of production limits.

Securities 49

New York: Today's securities market situation was stable at the opening but lacked momentum due to uncertainty in Washington and the brewing labor unrest in Detroit. 37,000 auto industry workers there are about to strike, but due to official intervention, it has not yet materialized. The securities market then became sluggish. Sentiment has not shown any significant decline, but there is no sign of breaking the speculative deadlock at present. Zhang Xueliang Goes to Nanchang to Meet Chiang 51

Shen Honglie, Tang Guozhen, and Others Accompany Him

Will Inspect Bandit Areas After Returning to Hankou

(Hankou) At 8:00 PM on the 7th, Zhang Xueliang, leading Tang Guozhen, Tan Hai, and others, took the Wu Xue steamer to Xunyang, then transferred to Jiangxi to meet Chiang. Shen Honglie accompanied him. Before his departure, Zhang told reporters that this trip to meet Chiang would last two or three days, and he would not go anywhere else. It is said that after returning to Hankou, he will still go to the bandit areas to inspect. Shen said that he would accompany Zhang to Jiangxi and, if time permitted, would return to Hankou once; otherwise, he would go to Nanjing. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang went to Jiangxi to meet Chiang to report on the military and political situation after taking office and to discuss the bandit suppression and aftermath in detail with Chiang. In addition to Shen Honglie accompanying him, He Zhuguo also went. Chiang is scheduled to convene a meeting of national division commanders in Jiangxi on the 15th for training. He Zhuguo is going to listen to the training because he is also a division commander. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Hankou) After Zhang Xueliang went to Jiangxi on the 7th, the headquarters affairs were handled by Qian Dajun on his behalf. Wan Fulin telegraphed that he would depart on the 6th and was expected to arrive in Hankou on the 8th. Yu Xuezhong turned south to Pingnan on the 7th and should arrive no later than the 10th. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong's trip to Hankou to meet Zhang did not materialize on the 7th because he received a telegram on the evening of the 6th that Zhang Xueliang had already gone to Nanchang to meet Commander-in-Chief Chiang. Yu plans to go after Zhang returns to Hankou. (Dispatch, 7th)

(Jinan) The division and brigade commanders have successively come to Jinan from their defense posts to go to Jiangxi for training. (Special dispatch, 7th)

The 36th Division Takes Over Defense of Quanzhou and Yongchun 52

(Xiamen) The 36th Division has taken over the defense of Quanzhou and Yongchun. The Fu and Li brigades have all arrived in Quanzhou, and on the 7th, they were assigned to defend various counties. The Li Brigade is stationed in Jinjiang, Nan'an, and Hui'an counties, with the brigade headquarters in Quanzhou. The Fu Brigade is stationed in Tong'an, Anxi, Yongchun, and Dehua counties. Li Chuying's brigade of the 83rd Division left Quanzhou for Tong'an on the 4th. Chen Wu's brigade left Hui'an for Tong'an via Quanzhou on the 6th and will succeed the 3rd Division in Longyan. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Xiamen) Provincial news: The Military Affairs Commission telegraphed that the 1st and 2nd Marine Brigades stationed in Fujian are under the control and dispatch of Chen Yi. Li Shijia has telegraphed to comply. The defense area of the marine troops is in Siming, Ningde, Luoyuan, Changle, Lianjiang, and coastal counties. Fujian Province is opening special taxes and has appointed Yang Tianyu and Chen Desen as the chief and deputy chiefs of the Xiamen Special Tax Branch. It is reported that the province can collect one million annually. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Chiang Orders He Jian to Suppress the Xiao and Gao Bandits by a Deadline 53

(Changsha) Chiang telegraphed He Jian, ordering him to suppress the Xiao and Gao bandits before the end of March. The Ministry of Finance Strictly Prohibits Private Issuance of Lottery Tickets 54

(Nanjing) Since the issuance of aviation lottery tickets, many unscrupulous merchants have taken the opportunity to establish various names and issue lottery tickets. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance specially telegraphed the provincial governments again, stating that all lottery tickets and similar lottery methods that have not been approved by the government should be strictly prohibited and ordered to be stopped immediately. They are not allowed to be advertised in newspapers so that the people can purchase aviation tickets as much as possible. (Special dispatch, 7th)

The Shandong Provincial Government and Industrial Circles Welcome the Shanghai Inspection Group 59

(Jinan) This morning, the Shanghai Industrial Inspection Group of 264 people arrived in Jinan. The various committee members, department heads, secretaries-general of the provincial government, and various trade associations all held flags to welcome them at the station. After getting off the train, they stayed at the Zhaotaiyan and Jiaoji hotels. According to Qian Chengxu, they accepted Han Fuqu's invitation to visit. Shandong's agricultural products are worth more than 250 million annually, ranking first in the country. This group hopes to cooperate with Shandong's industrial circles in production and sales, with cotton yarn being the most important. At noon, Han hosted the group at the provincial government. Han gave a welcoming speech, hoping that the group would pay attention to the Yellow River and Grand Canal water conservancy, and the gold mines of Muping and Yantai. Finally, he said that industry is the foundation of the country. Although the people are shouting about saving the country through aviation, our country currently has no gasoline. If there are two planes, the cost of gasoline and spare parts alone can transfer the country's money to foreign countries. Qian Chengxu gave a reply. Photos were taken, and the meeting was adjourned. In the afternoon, the group visited the pigment industry and flour industry. On the 8th, they will visit the electric, paper-making, match-making, and spinning industries. On the 9th, they will visit the agricultural experiment station, radio station, etc. At noon, they will host a return banquet for all circles. In the evening, the provincial government will host a farewell banquet. The group will go to Qingdao and Sichuan, Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Guangxi for inspection. (Special dispatch, 7th)

The Magistrate of Luoning County Was Executed by Firing Squad for Abandoning the City and Fleeing When the Liu Bandits Raided 60

(Kaifeng) Qin Shuo, the magistrate of Luoning County, abandoned the city and fled when the Liu Guitang bandits raided Luoning from Mianchi. He was arrested and sent to the pacification headquarters. It was found that the magistrate also served as the captain of the security team. When the Liu bandits raided on February 17, there were more than 500 soldiers in the city, and there was still defensive strength. He had previously received an order from the Tenth Administrative Inspectorate to defend the city to the death. However, Qin arbitrarily abandoned the city and fled through the west gate with his family and the strong men's team, causing the Liu bandits to enter the city without firing a shot, causing severe damage to the people. The pacification headquarters reported to Chairman Chiang, who approved the execution by firing squad in accordance with the regulations on rewards and punishments for civil and military officials and soldiers in the bandit suppression area. The pacification headquarters also notified the administrative inspectors and county magistrates of various districts to serve as a warning. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Unified Method for Post-Disaster Public Works Funds in Hebei, Shandong and Henan 69

(Nanjing) The three proposals for unified management of post-disaster public works funds in Hebei, Henan, and Shandong, formulated by the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association, have been approved by the Executive Yuan and submitted to the Economic Committee for review. The proposals are: 1. To follow the precedent of the Yellow River breach in the 14th year of the Republic, adding surcharges to railways, postal services, and shipping, with railway and shipping limited to passenger transport to avoid affecting commercial transport. 2. The governments of Henan, Shandong, and Hebei provinces will designate suitable collateral to issue bonds for the post-disaster water conservancy project to block the Yellow River breach. 3. In response to the request of the people's representatives of Hebei, the Economic Committee is requested to allocate some US cotton and wheat loans for subsidies. (7th Special Dispatch)

Preparation for the Sewerage Project in Nanjing 71

(Nanjing) The Dutch Boxer Indemnity is allocated for water conservancy in Nanjing. A Dutch engineer, Alma, has come to China to handle the sewerage project in the capital. The preparation period is tentatively set at nine months. The engineering plan includes organizing a survey team with a chief leading the overall operation, concurrently held by the chief engineer. It will be divided into four topographic survey teams, four hydrological survey teams, and two leveling teams. The topographic survey teams will map the urban and suburban areas, covering a total area of 100 square kilometers. The survey period will be six months. The hydrological survey teams will measure flow velocity and discharge, with the measurement range including the moat and the tributaries of the Qinhuai River, totaling approximately 39 kilometers in length. The measurement period will be approximately five months. The leveling teams will map the longitudinal sections of the city's major roads, the quantity of which will be determined after the sewerage drainage system is reviewed. The current estimated total length is approximately 200 kilometers. Budgeted expenses for the preparation of the sewerage project: (A) Topographic Survey Team: Mapping fee: 26,173 yuan; Salary: 19,902 yuan; Office expenses: 1,665 yuan; Equipment purchase: 1,870 yuan; Special public expenses: 2,736 yuan; (B) Hydrological Survey Team: Mapping fee: 17,825 yuan; Salary: 14,360 yuan; Office expenses: 960 yuan; Purchase fee: 585 yuan; Special public expenses: 1,920 yuan; (C) Leveling Team: Mapping fee: 7,386 yuan; Salary: 4,392 yuan; Office expenses: 800 yuan; Purchase fee: 1,330 yuan; Special public expenses: 864 yuan; (D) Survey fee: 2,000 yuan. (7th Special Dispatch)

Northern Fujian Circles' Rally for Bandit Suppression Cables Nationwide 90

Jian'ou: Northern Fujian circles' rally for bandit suppression cables nationwide, unanimously supporting Wang and Jiang's true telegram. The original telegram reads: "We humbly read the true telegram of Director Wang and Chairman Jiang. The words are earnest and sincere, and the sincerity of planning for the country shines through the past and present. The country's affairs are difficult, and it is now at its extreme. Saving the country and preserving its existence, there is no other way than suppressing bandits and building. In recent years, the central government's decisions have indeed been a blueprint for revival. Your Excellency is responsible for vigorously implementing it, using a kind and gentle spirit to seek the realization of unity. Your public-spiritedness and decisiveness are admired by all. Now that the country is full of hope for governance, local rebellion suddenly arises. Former ones like Feng and Fang, and recent ones like Chen and Li, do not hesitate to harm the liver and brains of the people to satisfy their own selfish desires. Fortunately, Your Excellency's command is decisive, and the deployment is well-organized, so that the chaos can be quickly quelled and the foundation of the country can be re-established. Now, after the Fujian rebellion has been quelled, we reiterate the essentials of saving the country, earnestly using the meaning of suppressing bandits as a temporary solution and construction as the fundamental solution, with the central and local governments being sincere and cooperative, to inform the people. Anyone with blood and qi will rise up. Northern Fujian has suffered from banditry frequently, and the people are extremely impoverished. The pain is deeply felt, and the excitement is even deeper. Today, people from all walks of life gathered in Yanping, and the entire audience unanimously decided to swear allegiance to Your Excellency, implement our propositions, and send this telegram for your review." Now that lost territories have not been recovered, foreign insults are becoming more urgent, and world disaster is approaching. Governance, chaos, survival, and extinction all depend on this. We hope that everyone will agree on propositions and work together to save the crisis. The party and the country are fortunate. Northern Fujian Circles' Rally for Bandit Suppression bows to you. Record of the Reception of Gubeikou 96

Chinese and Japanese Representatives Hold Grand Ceremony

Nearby Five Small Passes Also Received Simultaneously

Beiping Correspondence: The reception of Gubeikou was originally scheduled for the 18th of last month. Later, due to issues such as the replacement of Japanese troops and the failure of puppet organizations to relocate, it was slightly postponed and changed to today (the 4th) to begin the reception. At 11:30 AM today, Chinese and Japanese representatives and related personnel held a grand reception ceremony at the Gubeikou Administrative Commissioner's Office. At the same time, the heads of our various agencies, Liu Youxun, the director of the Gubeikou Zozhi Bureau, Huo Shi, the director of the office, and Guan Qinghua, the chief of the Public Security Branch Bureau, assumed their posts and received administrative and police powers. The Japanese and puppet police posts were completely withdrawn, and our police maintained local order. The nearby five small passes also began to be received. The details are recorded as follows:

Preparations 97

Both Chinese and Japanese Sides Have Agreed on All Procedures in Advance

The puppet organizations completed their work on the 2nd and moved to the foot of the Great Wall on North Street. All the houses were left for the use of our office, the Zozhi Bureau, and the Public Security Branch Bureau, and other agencies to work. Our receiving commissioner Yin Rugeng, accompanied by Wei Yonghe, commander of the Third Security Corps of the War Zone, Huo Shi, director of the Gubeikou Office of the Administrative Commissioner's Office, and Liu Youxun, director of the Gubeikou Zozhi Bureau, departed from Beiping at 7:30 AM on the 3rd, arrived in Miyun at 11:30 AM, took a short rest, and then went directly to Gubeikou with Qiu Heting, the magistrate of Miyun County, and Xu Shiying, the commander of the Second Security Brigade, arriving at around 3:00 PM. They first went to the Gubeikou office to prepare all reception matters. They then met with Yongan Houde, the commander of the 25th Regiment of the Japanese Army and the garrison commander of Gubeikou, and others, and agreed on everything. Immediately, personnel were dispatched to post notices in various townships, announcing the date of reception, so that the public would know. They also ordered the receiving police stationed in Shixia to arrive at Gubeikou this morning (the 4th) to maintain law and order.

Holding the Ceremony 98

After all preparations were completed, the reception was carried out this morning, the 4th. Japanese Commissioner in Charge of Handover Matsui and Kwantung Army Staff Officer Major General Sakagaki also arrived from Chengde this morning to handle the handover. At 11:30 AM, the reception ceremony was held. The participants on our side were Commissioner Yin Rugeng, Security Corps Commander Wei Yonghe, Gubeikou Office Director Huo Shi, Miyun County Magistrate Qiu Heting, Gubeikou Zozhi Bureau Director Liu Youxun, Gubeikou Public Security Branch Bureau Chief Guan Qinghua, Security Second Brigade Commander Xu Shiying, Gubeikou Chamber of Commerce President Zhou Hongen, Livelihood Association President Duan Liying, Post Office Director Zhang Bingzhong, Beiping Postal District Inspector Liu Guangqi, Gentry Ma Wensheng, First Primary School Principal Geng Xiangming, and others. The Japanese side included Matsui, Acting Director of the Kwantung Army Resident Chengde Special Service Agency, Kwantung Army Staff Officer Major General Sakagaki, Yongan, representative of the 7th Division, and Team Attached Sanqiao, Consul Matsuoka, etc., as well as Chinese and foreign guests, totaling more than 200 people. After raising the Blue Sky White Sun flag, 10,000 cannons were fired. The participants took their seats separately. First, our representative Yin Rugeng delivered a speech, "Today, we are holding the reception ceremony for the Gubeikou area. Chinese and foreign officials and people are gathered together. I am very happy to be personally involved in this matter. In the past, a committee was set up to handle the reception of the war zone. Now, this committee has been abolished. All unfinished reception matters are entrusted to the administrative supervisors of Luanyu-Jimiyun area under the instruction of the Executive Yuan's Resident Peace Political Reorganization Committee. Gubeikou is located in the Jimiyun area, so the reception procedures are my responsibility. It is only today that the reception is being implemented. Gubeikou is a major town in terms of geography and history. In recent years, the local area has prospered and made progress day by day. It is necessary to expand the original administrative organs. It has now been approved by the Hebei Provincial Government to establish the Gubeikou Zozhi Bureau, which is subordinate to Miyun County and assists the county government in handling local administrative affairs in Gubeikou. The Gubeikou Public Security Branch Bureau will also be reorganized so that it can effectively maintain law and order. As for foreign affairs, they will be handled by the director of the Gubeikou Office of the Administrative Supervisor of Jimiyun area, acting under my authority. In short, after the reception of Gubeikou, two new institutions will be added, one is the Zozhi Bureau, which handles local administrative affairs, and the other is the office, which handles foreign affairs. These two institutions will also be established and start working today. From today onwards, the local heads of agencies and local people must work together in harmony, each fulfilling their responsibilities, and strive to make the local area even more prosperous so that Chinese and foreign merchants can live and work in peace. This is what I hope," etc. Then, Miyun County Magistrate Qiu Heting, Huo Shi, Director of the New Office in Gubeikou, Liu Youxun, Director of the Zozhi Bureau, and Matsui, representative of the Japanese Kwantung Army, successively gave speeches.

Post-Meeting Feast 99

After the speeches, all the personnel took a group photo in front of the venue to commemorate the occasion. At around 12:00 PM, the ceremony ended and the meeting adjourned. Afterwards, our receiving commissioner Yin Rugeng hosted a banquet at the office to entertain the participants from both sides. The guests and hosts dispersed at around 1:00 PM. Yin is scheduled to return to Beiping on the 6th to report on the reception. Japanese representatives Matsui, Sakagaki, and others will return to Chengde tomorrow (the 5th).

Implementing the Reception 100

Gubeikou implemented the reception this morning (the 4th). The thirty-one police officers stationed in Shixia waiting for orders set out in two groups this morning to take over the defense. One group of twenty people set out from Shixia on foot at 6:00 AM this morning and arrived in Gubeikou at 9:00 AM, immediately setting up posts and watching. The positions of the Japanese and puppets were removed at the same time. Another group of eleven people, accompanied by Ma Xilin, councillor, and Han Jiasheng, branch director, set out from Gubeikou to the Caojialukou northeast of Gubeikou at 5:00 AM. They arrived at the pass at 10:00 AM and immediately took over the pass. The puppet organization in Gubeikou had moved to the foot of the Great Wall earlier. The houses they occupied were returned to our side and set up as the office, the Zozhi Bureau, and the Public Security Branch Bureau. Huo Shi, Liu Youxun, Guan Qinghua, and others took up their new positions and began to work after participating in the reception ceremony. The Administrative Commissioner's Office issued a notice to appease the people. The Zozhi Bureau Office and the Chief of the Public Security Branch Bureau also issued notices of taking office. The notice of the Administrative Commissioner's Office to appease the people is recorded below: "It is hereby announced that the Hebei Provincial Government has forwarded a letter from the Executive Yuan's Resident Beiping Political Reorganization Committee stating that the unfinished matters of receiving the counties in the war zone will be continued by the administrative supervisors of the Luan Yu Jimiyun areas of the province, etc. Following this, the outline of the methods for temporarily setting up administrative organs after the reception of Gubeikou was drafted and submitted to the Hebei Provincial Government for approval. Now, on February 28th of the 13th year of the Republic, the Gubeikou area will be received, and all administrative matters and local security will be handled separately by the Miyun County Government, the Gubeikou Zozhi Bureau, and the Gubeikou Public Security Branch Bureau. Foreign affairs will be handled by the Director of the Gubeikou Office of the Administrative Supervisor of Jimiyun area, acting under the authority of the Commissioner. In addition to separate royal letters and orders, it is hereby announced that all people of all walks of life are informed and must abide by laws and regulations and live in peace. This is of the utmost importance. This is hereby announced."

People Celebrate 101

The people of Gubeikou, hearing the news of the reception, were overjoyed to see the light of day again and were extremely happy. The entire city has raised the Blue Sky White Sun national emblem since the morning to celebrate. The streets and markets are bustling with people, cheering and dancing, expressing their joy. Lanterns and high-legged races were also held at night to express their celebration. (March 4th)
