Sichuan-Kang Expedition Team Reaches Ya'an on Southern Route 103

丨Qiong Bamboo Near Extinction Due to Destruction丨

Ya'an Correspondence from Shanghai Correspondent for the Sichuan-Kang Expedition Team: After spending the discarded lunar new year in Chengdu, the team split into southern and northern routes on the morning of February 19th. Zhang Xianmei, Chen Youqin, and Liu Sida, along with a delegation of Chengdu elders organized to inspect bandit areas, departed together for northern Sichuan. The reporter, along with Lu Yi, Wang Zhenhuan, and Su Dezheng, departed for southern Sichuan to begin on-site research into the Kang-Tibetan issue. There were also three temporary companions: Li Zhongying, the compilation director of the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Supervisory Office; Li Xiaxuan, a reporter for the Sichuan Construction Daily; and Huang Fanggang, a professor at Sichuan University. Some provided assistance along the way due to local hospitality, while others participated in the expedition in a personal capacity. The journey from Chengdu to Ya'an is 340 li (approximately 170 kilometers). Originally, there was a direct automobile road, but due to the unstable roadbed and frequent rains in the counties under Ya'an's jurisdiction, it was only passable to Qionglai. On that day, the automobile traveled 80 li from Mindu (Chengdu), crossing the Min River in Xinjin County, which was very dangerous. It took two hours to get back on the car. In the afternoon, around 4 o'clock, they arrived in Qionglai and stayed in a small inn. Pigsties and chicken coops were everywhere, and it was very dirty. There were no meals or blankets. Most inland inns in Sichuan are like this. The reporters managed to eat something and spread out their bedding to sleep. At this time, they felt the need to bring their own blankets. That night, they asked the innkeeper to hire porters to send them to Ya'an by sedan chair and contacted the garrison for transportation and relay at different stations. On the morning of the 20th, after washing up, they set off in sedan chairs, walking along the highway. They would occasionally lower the chairs to allow the porters to rest. Moreover, nine out of ten sedan chair porters had an opium addiction. After traveling 20 li, they had to indulge in opium. They would scatter into opium dens, stretch their legs and feet, and not care about the time. It was very difficult for the passengers to gather the porters to start the journey again. It seems that these sedan chair porters and opium have become a cyclical relationship. If they don't carry, they have no money for opium; if they don't indulge in opium, they have no strength to carry the sedan chair. It's pitiful, hateful, and beyond salvation. Qiongzhou is an important prefecture in western Sichuan, but it has a heavy burden and weak production, and there is no commercial activity to speak of. Other social conditions were not known in detail due to the hurried overnight stay during the journey. Qiongzhou is famous for its bamboo, which can be used for carving or making canes. According to local elders, it has become extinct due to the devastation of war and the destruction of bamboo shoot eaters. The Qionglai bamboo sold in other ports recently is produced in Yunshan, northern Sichuan and is an imitation. Leaving Qionglai City, the snowy peaks of Maoxian County can be seen in the distance, shining in the sunlight, like white clouds in summer and autumn. It is said that the snow on the Dapailing Mountain is several feet thick. From the foot of the mountain to the peak is 40 li, requiring a day's journey. When one is in this magnificent environment, it is even more sufficient to broaden one's mind. After traveling 80 li, they stayed overnight at a small inn in Baizhang. There is a place name on this road called Heizhuguan, located at the intersection of several counties. It is known as a place where bandits often appear. It was fortunate that the journey was peaceful that day. On the morning of the 21st, they set off from Baizhang and arrived at the county seat of Mingshan at noon. Mengshan Mountain outside the city is famous for its tea, called Mengding Tea, also known as "Water from the Yangtze River, Tea from the Top of Mengshan." From Mingshan, they started at Datangpu. A platoon of soldiers who had been escorting them turned back. The reporter and his party of seven bravely marched forward, passing the Jinjiguan Mountain slope, which was very steep. One man guarding the pass can block ten thousand people. It was said that there were also bandits appearing, but they were able to cross it safely. After passing this pass, the Ya River was in sight. After traveling another 20 li, they arrived at the outskirts of Ya'an, crossed the Ya River on a bamboo raft bridge, entered Ya'an City, climbed Cangping Mountain, and stayed at the private village of Yao Zhongliang, the director of the transportation department of the Sichuan-Kang Border Defense Army. Ya'an was originally a prefectural seat but was recently changed to a county seat. Tea production is the main industry and the only export product to Kang and Tibet. It is suitable for the diet and physical needs of Tibetans. They cannot live without it, otherwise, the butter, mutton, and highland barley in the Tibetan's stomach will cause bloating and death. It is an important commodity in Han-Tibetan trade relations. The climate is rainy. There is a saying that "a light breeze brings rain, and Rongjing is arid." Qingxi was the original name, now changed to Hanxi, because it is at the foot of Jiaoxiang Ridge, so it is windy all day long. Rongjing, like the northern plateau, is also west of Ya'an. Because Xiangling Mountain stands tall, there is little rain all year round. Like a huge wave in the Pacific Ocean, the westward wind is blocked by the lofty Xiangling Mountain, and after changes in air pressure, it rains, just in Ya'an, causing Ya'an to have more rain, Hanyuan to have more wind, and Rongjing to suffer from drought, hence this saying. The reporter, being in this situation, encountered rain every day, and even more believed it to be true. The social and commercial conditions of Ya'an are described in detail below.

(1) Farmland: According to the measurement in the sixth year of the Yongzheng reign (1728), the area of farmland is 70,000 mu plus a fraction, and the area of land is 10,000 mu plus a fraction. (Population): According to the county government's statistics in the twelfth year (1734), there were 33,000 households in the whole county, with a population of 130,000, including 74,000 men and 57,000 women.

(1) Land Tax: The poll tax is over 4,300 taels of silver. Twenty-one years ago (1912), the silver tax was 30,000 yuan.

(1) Climate: According to the report of the First Agricultural Farm of the Sichuan-Kang Border Area Colonization Command in the 21st year (1932), the temperatures in Fahrenheit are: January 43, February 42, March 62, April 65, July 82, August 78, September 67, October 64, November 60, December 41.

(1) Tea Industry: Statistics on the production of border tea: In the early years of the Republic, 50,000 yin (a unit of weight), each yin containing 5 packets of tea, each packet weighing 20 jin (approximately 10 kilograms), totaling 5,000,000 jin (approximately 2,500 metric tons). In the 12th year of the Republic (1923), 40,000 yin, each yin containing 5 packets of tea, each packet weighing 19 jin, totaling 3,800,000 jin. In the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), 40,000 piao (another unit), each piao containing 5 packets of tea, each packet weighing 17 jin, totaling 3,400,000 jin. The annual surtax is set at 50,000 piao, and 5,000,000 jin of tea should be handled. The tea that falls short of each piao must be collected and transported from Ebian and Jiading areas.

(1) Fu Tea (Stomach Tea): 50 piao, each piao containing 500 jin of tea, totaling 25,000 jin.

(1) Value of Border Tea: In the early years of the Republic, the market price in Ya'an was 8.0 yuan per piao, with a total value of 400,000 yuan. The price in Kangding was 14 yuan, with a total value of 700,000 yuan. In the 12th year of the Republic (1923), the price in Ya'an was 5.0 yuan, with a total value of 200,000 yuan. The price in Kangding was 14 yuan, with a total value of 560,000 yuan. In the 21st year of the Republic (1932), the price in Ya'an was 3 yuan, with a total value of 170,000 yuan. The price in Kangding was 14 yuan, with a total value of 560,000 yuan. The price of tea in Ya'an is decreasing day by day, and the income of tea farmers is becoming thinner and thinner. As the tea merchants' tax burden increases day by day, they secretly reduce the quantity of tea leaves in each packet and mix in inferior tea to deceive the barbarians. Therefore, sales are not as prosperous as in the past. The current government has strictly prohibited adulteration and is trying to remedy the situation.

(1) Tea Tax: The tax and surtax on each border tea ticket is 1.7 yuan, and the tax and surtax on each fu tea ticket is 10.0 yuan.

(1) Salt: The annual amount of salt in Ya'an is about 2,600,000 jin. The amount of salt consumed by the people of Ya'an is only 120,000 jin. Assuming an average annual salt consumption of 3 jin per person, the 100,000 adults should consume 300,000 jin. That is, half of the people have no salt to eat.

(1) Cloth: In the early years of the Republic of China, Hubei cloth was used exclusively, known as "Riguang Cloth." At that time, there were more than a dozen cloth shops from Shaanxi. Later, due to high taxes and prices, local cloth from Hongya and Jiajiang rose and seized the market. According to estimates by more than a dozen commercial firms, the value of imports in the early years of the Republic of China was more than 300,000 yuan. In the 20th year of the Republic of China (1931), the value of imports was more than 800,000 yuan, and about 100,000 yuan was distributed to the people of Ya'an.

(1) Cloth Tax: A package of local cloth from Hongya and Jiajiang contains 12 pi (a unit of length), and each pi weighs 1 jin. Each package from Hongya to Ya'an was taxed 3 jiao in the 19th year (1930), 5 jiao in the 21st year (1932), and 8 jiao in the 22nd year (1933). The Hongya Customs also includes the anti-communist suppression fee.

(1) Rice: Annual production is about 56,000 shi (a unit of volume).

(1) Corn: Annual production is 50,000 shi. Based on the current population and food consumption, there is a shortage of more than 20,000 shi per year, which is worth more than 300,000 yuan at the current market price. (National News Agency)

Lawsuit Regarding the Medicinal Properties of Ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum 104

Are the Medicinal Properties Incompatible?

Lawyers Engage in Extensive Debate

Jinan Correspondence: Recently, Wang Shilang, a third-generation doctor in Qingdao, used the traditional Chinese medicine ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum to treat a woman after childbirth. A few days later, the woman died. The woman's family sued the doctor for not knowing the medicinal properties and being negligent of human life. The Qingdao court sentenced him to a fine of 100 yuan. The doctor refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Shandong High Court. Today (the 5th), the debate has concluded, and a date has been set for the verdict. The doctor hired lawyer Zhou Feng to defend him, citing many ancient books, claiming that the two medicines are not contradictory. This case involves the debate on the medicinal properties in our country and is quite interesting. Therefore, the process is recorded as follows.

How it Happened 105

Wang Shilang, a native of Rizhao County, is 46 years old and a third-generation doctor. He currently runs the Kailan Pharmacy at No. 64 Jinxiang Road, Hou Guan, Qingdao, and also practices medicine. On August 21st of last year, Hou Xueyi came to his pharmacy and said that his wife was seriously ill after childbirth and asked him to come for treatment. After Wang went, he saw that the patient, Zhang, Hou's wife, had blood stasis after childbirth, had a severe headache, and was also suffering from an external cold. He was very dangerous, so he followed the ancient prescription Siwu Shenghua Tang, plus ginseng, Feces Trogopterorum, and mustard charcoal to treat her. After taking it, she was still quite safe. Later, due to a quarrel between the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law, the illness worsened. Moreover, the patient took Western medicine aspirin tablets to sweat and ate a lot of watermelon, which aggravated the illness. He also invited Zhang, the director of the Huidong Pharmacy, to check. Zhang said that she had ruptured her water gate after childbirth and performed surgery three times without success. She died at 7 pm on the 26th. The deceased's family was poor and delayed the funeral. Zhao said that the medicine taken by the deceased had contradictory ingredients. Hou Xueyi, the husband of the deceased, and Hou Liu, his mother, suspected that the doctor Wang Shilang had used the wrong medicine, causing the death. They filed a negotiation with Dr. Wang. The two sides held their own opinions and could not resolve it. Hou Liu filed a lawsuit in the local court, requesting a judgment according to law.

Prosecution in Court 106

After Hou Liu filed the lawsuit, the prosecutor examined the body and found that she died of illness, and the case was dismissed. Hou Liu filed another lawsuit. Prosecutor Mi Xian conducted a detailed investigation and asked You Xiaoting to testify in court. He also sent a letter to the Social Bureau to ask a Chinese medicine doctor to identify the prescription, believing that it had no monarch-minister-assistant-guide composition, had shallow knowledge, and misused ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum, causing the death of the person. He should be prosecuted for the crime under Article 290, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. After being tried by Judge Liu Zhenhan, the debate ended, and he was sentenced to a fine of 100 yuan according to law. If the fine is converted into imprisonment, it will be calculated at 0.2 yuan per day according to Article 55, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law. Before the judgment is finalized, he will not be detained and there is no need to notify him of the discount. That is, the judgment was made in accordance with Article 315 of the Criminal Procedure Law, and the appeal conference was designated as the Shandong High Court, with a deadline of ten days, after which it would be invalid.

Appeal 107

After the verdict was pronounced, the defendant Wang Shilang refused to accept the verdict of guilt of causing death due to negligence in business and hired lawyer Zhou Feng in Jinan to file an appeal to the High Court, requesting a retrial. The reasons he held were four: (1) The combination of ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum is the only main medicine following an ancient prescription for treating blood stasis after childbirth. There is evidence from Lei Gong's Materia Medica and the Compendium of Materia Medica and the cases of famous scholars. These books and cases all say that ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum treat the disease, and they are feared but not feared. If there is a disease, there must be a medicine for it. Treating from the opposite direction, each has its own considerations. The blood stasis after childbirth cannot be opened without Feces Trogopterorum. However, at that time, the Qi is extremely weak, and it cannot be consolidated without the great strength of ginseng. Even if it is truly feared, it is only that ginseng is useless in the medicine. How can it be said that it is inappropriate? (2) The original trial said that the illness worsened after taking the medicine, which was a one-sided slander by Hou Liu and cannot be adopted. Neighbors and You Xiaoting should be investigated. You Xiaoting also said in the original trial that Feces Trogopterorum is feared but not feared, and this medicine should be used to treat this disease. Hou Xueyi said that the prescription was criticized by Zhao, but he was repeatedly summoned to court. You Xiaoting testified in court that the medicine was right for her disease, and there are records to prove it. (3) The prescription should be identified by a responsible doctor with high moral character and rich knowledge. If there is any disagreement, it must be debated in court. The case said that the appraiser said that the prescription has no monarch-minister-assistant-guide composition, which is even more unfounded. The angelica, chuanxiong, black ginger, and peach kernels in the prescription are the monarch, as well as donkey-hide gelatin are the assistant, the ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum are the guide, mustard is the minister, licorice harmonizes the ingredients, and everyone is considered. Without investigating the condition, it cannot be said that the medicine is not right. What's more, the condition and the medicine are perfectly matched? (4) For Hou Zhang's illness, the hospital must be investigated, and President Zhang and his female doctor from Huidong Pharmacy must be summoned. However, President Zhang was not asked, and the valueless words of You Xiaoting were believed, which is unreasonable. In addition, there are four pieces of irrefutable evidence. The appeal is for the court to determine innocence.

End of Debate 108

After receiving the application, the High Court held a hearing at 9 am on the 5th by Gao Xiansuo, the presiding judge of the Third Criminal Division. Lawyer Zhou Feng defended the defendant, saying that whether the defendant Wang Shilang committed the crime of causing death due to negligence depends on whether the ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum in the prescription are contradictory medicines, and whether the combination of the two can cause death. According to the Compendium of Materia Medica, in the section of mutually reinforcing, mutually dependent, mutually fearing, and mutually antagonizing medicines in the preface and the lower part, ginseng is listed as fearing Feces Trogopterorum, and Feces Trogopterorum is listed as hating ginseng. However, the 36 kinds of medicines listed in the contradictory medicines section do not include these two ingredients. This is irrefutable evidence that they are not contradictory. Furthermore, in the Compendium of Materia Medica, in the section on mountain herbs, the annotation of ginseng says that ancient prescriptions used Siwu Tang to treat closed menstruation, adding ginseng and Feces Trogopterorum, which means fearing but not fearing. Since ginseng fears but does not fear Feces Trogopterorum, Feces Trogopterorum also hates but does not hate ginseng. The combination of these two ingredients will not cause death. This is also irrefutable evidence. Also, in Yan Chunxi's "Methods for Childbirth and Postpartum," and Zhang Shiwan's "Medical Understanding of Postpartum," all cases of fever, headache, and abdominal pain after childbirth are treated with Sheng Hua Tang with modifications. If the patient has been ill for a long time and is weak, ginseng is added. If the pain does not stop, Feces Trogopterorum is added. If there are other symptoms, other medicines are added. Hou Zhang's illness was blood stasis after childbirth combined with wind and cold, causing fever, headache, and abdominal pain, and had been going on for 20 days, making her body weak. The defendant prescribed Sheng Hua Tang plus ginseng, Feces Trogopterorum, mustard, charcoal, and other ingredients, which was based on the established methods in various books and was the right medicine for the symptoms. Where is the mistake? This is also irrefutable evidence. Furthermore, Zhang, the president of Huidong Pharmacy, a Western doctor in Qingdao, diagnosed the disease as poor delivery during childbirth, tearing the small intestine and water gate, which is called "drawing intestinal wind." The defendant is a Chinese medicine doctor and has no surgical examination for this type of disease. However, since it is said that the small intestine and water gate are torn, there must be swelling, injury, and blood stasis at the torn area. Then, the defendant's Sheng Hua Tang with added ingredients for promoting blood circulation is also correct for this type of disease. This is also irrefutable evidence. Based on the above irrefutable evidence, combined with the patient's condition at that time, the patient's death was caused by poor delivery during childbirth, and by eating watermelon and taking aspirin arbitrarily after taking the medicine to cause sweating and aggravate the weakness, rather than by taking the defendant's prescription. The reasons are clear and understandable. At 11 o'clock, President Gao announced the end of the debate and adjourned the court for sentencing. (5th)

Jiangsu Farmers' Bank's Agricultural Economic Relief Plan 109

Actively Promoting After Restructuring

The Farmers' Bank of Jiangsu Province has been established for five years. Over the years, the business has progressed. The current paid-in capital has reached 1.6 million yuan, and there are 24 branches. It is an important bank in our country for rescuing the rural economy and is highly valued by all parties. Since the provincial government appointed Zhao Dihua as the general manager, in order to seek to expand the practical effects of relieving farmers, he has strived to develop and reform the bank's affairs. The reporter, considering that the bank is particularly important at a time when the rural economy is declining, paid a special visit to the authorities, and he was informed of the recent handling situation, which is recorded as follows.

Since January of this year, in order to concentrate resources and facilitate the allocation of funds, the bank has abolished the regional jurisdiction system and switched to the head office business. As a result, the business has become more developed than before. The achievements of the bank's "lending," "depositing," and "collecting" activities were compared between the total number in January of this year and the average number from July to the end of December of the previous year. "Lending" increased by about 25%, "ordinary deposits" increased by about 19%, and "savings deposits" increased by about 17%. A total of deposits increased by 450,000 yuan within a month, and "collection" decreased by 8%. In order to actually develop the farmers' economy, increase its own strength, and facilitate the financing of production, transportation, and other cooperative societies, the bank is actively promoting farmers' savings and the implementation of rural town remittance. At the same time, the bank felt that the business center of the province is organized farmers, that is, cooperative societies, but cooperative societies in Jiangsu Province often only have a nominal existence and lack practical effects. Therefore, it actively promotes rectification so that cooperative societies can also engage in production, transportation, sales, purchasing, utilization, and other businesses, which is sufficient to actually increase agricultural production. Recently, the bank also established a "Jiangsu Provincial Cooperative Agricultural Products Marketing Office" in Nanshi, Shanghai. Its task is to act as an agent for cooperatives or farmers in transporting and selling agricultural products and purchasing fertilizers, seeds, and other necessities. It has already begun to accept commissions from cooperatives in various places, and the work is extremely busy. Through this promotion, the bank can solve the entire process from sowing to product sales for farmers. This can actually promote agricultural production. The bank's new plan can be fully implemented this year, and the agricultural economy in Jiangsu Province will have considerable results.

Taicang 112

Playing with Dragon Lanterns Almost Caused a Disaster

Since the abolition of the lunar new year, flower drum operas, dragon lanterns, and large gambling venues have become increasingly popular in our county. Because the authorities did not investigate and prohibit them, people in society have been complaining. Around 9 pm the day before yesterday, dragon lanterns from Yutian Wang Temple and other places were playing in the streets. When they arrived at the flower drum opera venue opened by Shao Zengfu on Xinji River, they played dragon lanterns by beating gongs and drums. Shao Zengfu, the owner of the venue, thought that the gongs and drums were shaking the sky and interfering with the order of the venue, so he stepped forward to stop them, but it was ineffective and took away the gong. This aroused public anger and they carried the dragon lanterns into the venue and played them, smashing 20 teapots. The order was suddenly chaotic, and the general audience fled in all directions. Doors and windows were crushed. Fortunately, the Public Security Bureau received the news early and immediately ordered the squad leader to take the police to the venue to suppress them, so that no major disaster occurred.

Regular Dredging of Fushan Pond in Changshu 113

Fushan Pond in our county is an important passage to the Yangtze River. Later, due to the influx of tides, silt accumulated over the years. In addition, there has been a drought recently, and the river water is shallow and only two feet deep, making it difficult for ships to pass through. The Dredging Committee has decided and dredged it. Now, Hu Zhenkang, the chief of the twelfth district, has been appointed as the director, and Jin Ping, the chief of the eighth district, and Cheng Zhaoxiang, the chief of the first district, have been appointed as the deputy directors. After building a dam on the 10th of this month, construction will begin.

Wuxi Small Car Owners Call for Relief 114

The Xiyi Provincial Road has been completed and is scheduled to hold a opening ceremony in Wuxi on the 10th of this month. Jiangnan Automobile Company has signed an exclusive operating right agreement with the Construction Department. After the road is open to traffic, the company will collect road maintenance donations for all small cars traveling on the Xiyi Road. Two yuan will be charged for each round trip between Wuxi and Yixing. Small car companies heard this news that the fares set by long-distance buses are only one cent per Chinese li, so the single fare from Wuxi to Yixing is only 1.1 yuan, and the fare from Wuxi to Meiyuan is only two jiao. The selling price is extremely cheap, and the tax collection is extremely heavy. Small car companies will inevitably perish. The small car companies specially appointed representatives to request relief from the Construction Bureau and put forward three points: (1) Please reduce the road maintenance donation on Xiyi Road to 1 yuan. (2) Small cars are allowed to carry passengers from Yixing back to Wuxi. (3) The Jiangnan long-distance bus must not set up stops and sell tickets in Meiyuan. Zhang Dezai, the director of the Construction Bureau, agreed to contact Jiangnan Automobile Company to discuss the plan.

Fire in Jiangyin Lane Kills Many 115

Dashuxia Jiangyin Lane is a bustling market in the northern district, with shops lined up. Yesterday (the 7th) morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the rattan shop next to the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. At that time, the northeast wind was strong, and it was also midnight. The fire was fierce and quickly spread, burning four shops, including Xinshengxing Flower and Firecracker Shop and Grocery Store, across the street (and the house of resident Wang Yaoxi was also completely burned). A total of more than 20 houses were burned, and the loss was extremely heavy. After the fire broke out in the rattan shop, there was no back door, resulting in the burning of six men, women, and children, and two seriously injured. Fortunately, the Farmers' Bank was next door and was able to provide rescue, so it was not affected, which was a fortunate thing.

Dispute over the Opening of Xiyi Road 116

Jiangnan Automobile Company previously signed a contract with the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department to exclusively operate on the Xiyi Provincial Road and was scheduled to hold a opening ceremony on the 10th of this month and officially open to traffic on the 11th. The company has also determined the fare and other information, which has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the company also stipulates that ordinary business small cars must pay a road maintenance donation of 2 yuan per trip to Yixing. If they start from Guanxing and drive to Wuxi, they cannot carry passengers and can only return empty to avoid hindering the company's business. After hearing the news, the small car companies felt that the burden was too heavy, and the business would be completely deprived. The restriction on carrying passengers on the return trip would put the small cars to death. The fare set by Jiangnan Company is also too profitable, and the small cars will have no way to survive. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, representatives such as Cao Xuemei and Yang Zhiguang and more than a dozen others went to the County Construction Bureau with a document to petition for relief. Zhang Dezai, the director of the bureau, personally met with them. The representatives explained their business difficulties and requested (1) that the road maintenance donation on the Xiyi Road be reduced to 1 yuan per trip, (2) that passengers be allowed to be transported from Yixing back to Wuxi, (3) that the Jiangnan Automobile be allowed to stop and sell tickets from Wuxi Station to Meiyuan so that tourists can take small cars. Director Zhang agreed to contact Jiangnan Company and then discuss relief measures. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Kong Xiangrong Elaborates on the Yellow River Disaster Relief Work All Projects in Three Provinces Expected to Be Completed by the End of Next Month 125

Regarding the disaster relief work of the Yellow River Water Disaster Committee, yesterday morning, a reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Mr. Kong Xiangrong, the director of the disaster relief work group of the committee. According to him, the Yellow River disaster relief work in the three provinces will be fully completed by the end of next month. Mr. Kong took the night train to Beijing last night to meet with Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi and planned to visit the disaster area again for inspection. The details of his talk are recorded as follows.

All Projects to Be Completed Next Month According to Mr. Kong, the disaster relief work in the first district (i.e., Henan) and the third district (i.e., Shandong) of the Yellow River disaster area has been fully completed one after another. However, the disaster relief work in the second district (i.e., Hebei) is still in progress. Because the breach in this district is relatively large, it is difficult to block, and the lack of materials such as bricks and stones makes the work particularly difficult. However, this work cannot be delayed, so materials have been ordered from various places and will be concentrated in the Shijiazhuang area within 20 days, and then the blocking will continue, with the goal of completely completing all projects in the three provinces by the end of next month. 126

Materials for Blocking Breaches Arrive Mr. Kong continued to say that the breach in Shijiazhuang, Hebei, is relatively large, and the blocking work is naturally difficult. The work of hiring laborers to block the breach has already completed most of it. The breach-blocking project is not at the Shuikoumen, but in the villages on the high ground inside the Shuikoumen. A dike 25 meters high has been built, but this height is still not enough to stop the high floodwaters of the Yellow River, so it has been decided to continue to raise it by 10 meters. However, due to the lack of materials, it is estimated that another 3,500 cubic meters of stone, 100,000 bricks, 1.9 million sacks, 40 tons of steel wire, and 200 iron anchors are needed. But there is not much in stock at the front, so we have to wait for the materials to be transported before continuing. Yesterday, a telegram arrived in Shanghai stating that 500 cubic meters of large stones had been transported to Shijiazhuang, and a large batch of materials could be completely concentrated at Lanfeng Station within days, so I have telegraphed the local staff to quickly increase the number of vehicles and shifts from Lanfeng to Shijiazhuang to facilitate transportation. As for the breach-blocking work, when I went to inspect it, I gave instructions in person that blocking the breach should not wait for the water to recede, but should be carried out during the rising tide, which can use the water power to increase the working force. Therefore, I have telegraphed the upstream water affairs agencies that when the upstream water rises, they should immediately notify Shijiazhuang and other places by urgent telegram, and then calculate the time to start working, which will be easier. 127

Proposed Measures Approved by the Executive Yuan The Yellow River disaster has occurred frequently and is not uncommon. It has occurred almost every few years in recent years, and the people on both sides of the river who have been victimized are countless. Therefore, fundamental relief is necessary to achieve success. I have reported the situation to Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi and proposed three measures: (1) Add a Yellow River disaster relief fee to railway passenger tickets in Shandong, Hebei, and Henan provinces; (2) Stipulate Yellow River disaster relief funds in the three provinces; (3) Request the National Economic Council to allocate funds from the American cotton and wheat loan funds. The above three measures have been formally approved by the Executive Yuan meeting. 128

Yesterday Returned to the Construction Site to Direct the Work After briefly arranging important group affairs in Shanghai, Director Kong took the night train to Beijing last night and then went to the Changyuan construction site to direct the work. I found a copy of his telegram to the two supervisors Yu and Shao of the Supervisory Yuan, and the engineering bureau, which is attached below. "To the two Supervisors Yu and Shao in Kaifeng, and Engineer Song of the Engineering Office and Director Sun: I have been in internal meetings four times and traveled between Beijing and Shanghai every day without stopping. Fortunately, the three methods for raising 14 million yuan for the post-disaster water control project in the three provinces have been submitted by this committee to the Executive Yuan for submission to the administrative meeting, which was passed yesterday, and a letter has been sent to the National Economic Commission. I will hear the details with attention. Also, Rong came to Shanghai this morning to withdraw money and remit it to Bian, and will return to the construction site by night train, and plans to go to Lanfeng and Zhengzhou to urge the transportation of stone materials, and discuss the matter of adding trains on the Longhai Railway. A method for raising funds for the Hebei project has been agreed upon, and funds for repairing the embankment in Shijiazhuang are available. I especially inform Director Sun of this news for his comfort. Chairman Liu also telegraphed Rong to borrow funds for construction projects, or to stay in Beijing for half a day to visit Minister Kong to discuss matters. As for the finalization of the construction method for the closure, I think that Engineer Song has discussed it with Directors Sun and Yang. When Rong returns to the construction site, he will convene an engineering meeting, and when the materials are ready, he must seize the opportunity to rush to block the breach to achieve success. Kong Xiangrong, Director of the Disaster Relief Group, Yang." 129

National Goods Shipped to Sichuan Dispute British Ships Can Sail to Wanxian The Painful History of the Past Massacre Will Disappear Invisibly Today 130

The rise in water levels in the Sichuan River has caused opposition from foreign cargo handlers, who have unanimously stopped loading domestic goods into Sichuan and have also negotiated with the shipping company authorities. Now the freight rates for shipping domestic goods to Sichuan have been reduced, but the Hakka merchants are still dissatisfied and will promote the resumption of Japanese ships. The long-unresolved Wanxian Massacre will disappear invisibly in this price increase dispute, which is why the people of Sichuan are very dissatisfied. The latest news is detailed below.

Hakka Merchants Continue to Negotiate Foreign cargo handlers, because the freight rates set by various shipping companies on the Sichuan River are too high, have decided to petition the Social Affairs Bureau to suppress this unreasonable price. This price increase is entirely based on the people's livelihood, so the Hakka merchants continue to negotiate with the Minsheng Shipping Company. The Minsheng Shipping Company authorities, in view of the breakdown of the merchants' demands, also deeply know that the pricing was not carefully graded. They are afraid that a prolonged strike will hurt both sides, so the company took the initiative to make concessions and agreed to the foreign cargo handlers' request to reduce freight rates. 131

Reduce Freight Rates for Domestic Goods Li, a representative of the Minsheng Shipping Company, convened representatives of Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Sanbei, Jiejang, and other companies at the Jiejang Company the day before yesterday for another meeting to discuss freight rates for shipping domestic goods to Sichuan and agreed to reduce them. The result of the discussion was that all foreign goods, originally priced at 80 yuan per ton, would be reduced by 10 yuan and charged only 70 yuan. The foreign cargo handlers, after receiving the news, also convened a meeting of their members and decided that the reduction was too small. The merchants decided that each ton of foreign goods would only be charged 30 yuan for freight. If the shipping company does not agree, they can add another 10 yuan, so that both parties have not reached a satisfactory resolution. 132

Stop Shipping and Wait for Opportunities This matter has been under negotiation for several days, and there is still no definite solution. The Hakka merchants are now in the process of stopping the shipment of goods and have decided to take a wait-and-see attitude until the shipping bureau can sympathize. The water level in the Sichuan River is rising daily, and Japanese shipping companies in Shanghai are indeed planning to resume Sichuan River liner services. At the latest, in three weeks, Japanese ships can resume sailing to Chongqing. At that time, loading on Japanese ships will definitely get extremely low freight rates, so that the cost of goods shipped can be reduced by half compared to the current loading. 133

Wanxian Massacre Disappears Wanxian produces a large amount of tung oil every year, which is usually shipped to Shanghai by foreign merchant ships and then transferred to the United States. Since the Wanxian Massacre, British merchant ships such as Taikoo and Jardine Matheson have not been allowed to sail there. The goods from Wanxian have been obtained by our Chinese merchant ships. British merchants have repeatedly discussed resuming navigation with the Sichuan authorities, but they have not sympathized. This time, Minsheng and others advocated an alliance and allowed British ships to share the cargo transportation in Wanxian, which not only broke the exclusive business of Chinese merchant ships, but also caused the results of the Wanxian Massacre to disappear invisibly. After the implementation of this alliance treaty, British ships have achieved a great victory and are very satisfied. However, a certain shipping company in this port received a telegram from Sichuan stating that when this news reached Sichuan, the people of Sichuan were very dissatisfied. 134

Post and Telegraph Bureaus Merged to Operate from the 15th Expenditures After the Merger Must Not Exceed the Original Number 135

Central News Agency reports that in order to save expenses, facilitate the public, and increase transportation efficiency, the Ministry of Communications has issued an order to merge all post and telegraph bureaus below the third class. Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hebei provinces will be the first to pilot this. After observing the results, it will be extended to other regions. According to Zhu Menghou, director of the General Affairs Department of the Postal Administration, the issue of merging post and telegraph bureaus below the third class has now been decided and will be piloted in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hebei provinces starting on March 15th. Before the merger is implemented, it is still necessary to investigate what difficulties there may be in the merger, whether the lease contracts for the buildings have expired, and what troubles there may be in terminating the contracts. If there are no difficulties, the merger will be implemented on March 5th. For areas with difficulties, the merger will be implemented after the difficulties are resolved. The only principle of the post and telegraph merger is that the expenditures after the merger must not exceed the original number before the merger. As for the administration and business of other post and telegraph bureaus after the merger, they will remain independent and will not be merged.

Tung Oil Exports Have Increased Sharply in Recent Years From 400,000 Piculs to More Than 1 Million Piculs Valued at 405,701,269 Yuan 137

Chinese tung oil is of good quality and is highly praised by paint manufacturers in Europe and America. Therefore, foreign trade has improved in recent years. According to a survey by the International Trade Bureau, since the founding of the Republic of China, annual exports have increased from 400,000 piculs to more than 1 million piculs, valued at 405,701,269 yuan. The total exports for each year are recorded as follows: Year 1: 582,815 piculs, valued at 8,734,806 yuan; Year 2: 463,647 piculs, valued at 6,002,254 yuan; Year 3: 438,867 piculs, valued at 5,604,412 yuan; Year 4: 31,344 piculs, valued at 4,518,514 yuan; Year 5: 515,173 piculs, valued at 8,267,127 yuan; Year 6: 401,361 piculs, valued at 7,258,862 yuan; Year 7: 488,852 piculs, valued at 8,963,889 yuan; Year 8: 613,455 piculs, valued at 11,941,452 yuan; Year 9: 540,716 piculs, valued at 10,105,787 yuan; Year 10: 419,549 piculs, valued at 8,199,645 yuan; Year 11: 745,565 piculs, valued at 16,332,195 yuan; Year 12: 836,897 piculs, valued at 26,216,130 yuan; Year 13: 896,038 piculs, valued at 26,572,070 yuan; Year 14: 894,03 piculs, valued at 26,173,156 yuan; Year 15: 748,184 piculs, valued at 22,443,470 yuan; Year 16: 910,294 piculs, valued at 32,956,421 yuan; Year 17: 1,094,299 piculs, valued at 34,953,332 yuan; Year 18: 1,069,650 piculs, valued at 35,279,553 yuan; Year 19: 1,167,255 piculs, valued at 45,820,208 yuan; Year 20: 818,874 piculs, valued at 28,362,075 yuan; Year 21: 802,769 piculs, valued at 22,299,005 yuan; Year 22: 582,815 piculs, valued at 8,734,806 yuan. The total is 15,214,1492 piculs, worth a total of 405,701,269 yuan.

New Telephones Installed at the North Railway Station The original telephone exchange at the Shanghai North Railway Station was destroyed in the January 28th Incident two years ago. Later, to facilitate public affairs, 14 telephones from the American Shanghai Telephone Company were installed at the North Railway Station, the North Locomotive Depot, the McLean Road Station, and the Wusong Machine Factory. However, the efficiency was low and the cost was high, which was uneconomical. Therefore, a plan to install a full set of exchange equipment was submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval. 8,100 yuan was paid to Siemens Electric Factory to sign a contract to undertake the work. It is planned to install 10 pairs of trunk lines in the North Railway Station area, one exchange, one switchboard at the North Railway Station information desk, 28 extensions, 16 extensions in the North Locomotive Factory area, 4 extensions in the McLean Road Station area, one exchange in the Wusong Machine Factory, and 13 extensions. The system was put into use on March 1st. Since the installation of this exchange, the monthly recurring expenses are no more than 600 yuan (that is, even if it is expanded to 80 extensions in the future, it will only be 600 yuan), which is 500 yuan less than the previous 1,100 yuan spent monthly for only 14 extensions. This saves about 6,000 yuan per year. 138

Municipal Authorities Plan the City's Traffic Network, Starting with South Shanghai Central News Agency reports that the South Shanghai Bus Company, affected by the January 28th Incident, suffered excessive losses and was unable to maintain operations, declaring liquidation. However, since the ceasefire in South Shanghai, the city has become more prosperous than before. It is reported that the Municipal Public Works Bureau has recently implemented a loan with the foreign company "Asia Development," starting with South Shanghai first, and then extending to the entire city. The detailed information is recorded as follows. 139

Land and Water Routes The transportation network planned by the municipal authorities was originally to be carried out on both land and water routes. In terms of waterways, it has been carefully managed by Tan Boying, director of the ferry management office of the Xingye Trust Company, and it is now quite large in scale. As for land routes, after the closure of the South Shanghai Bus Company, the Municipal Public Works Bureau planned to take it over and operate it, starting with South Shanghai first, and then connecting it to West Shanghai and North Shanghai. This plan was ultimately unable to be realized early due to limited funding. 140

Negotiating Loans The Municipal Public Works Bureau believes that the suspension of the South Shanghai Bus Company was mostly due to the mismanagement of the operators, so it has repeatedly petitioned the municipal government to take it over and operate it. The municipal government once handed it over to the Finance Bureau, etc., to review and sign opinions, but the municipal treasury was severely strained due to the impact of the January 28th Incident. The Municipal Public Works Bureau's plan could not be realized, so Director Xu Peihuang negotiated a loan with the foreign company Asia Development, which was still to be operated by the bureau. The company agreed that all vehicles would be supplied by the company, and the company would operate on the circular road around the city and the route from West Gate to Longhua. After about three years, the loan would be repaid annually from the surplus. 141

Starting Preparations After the Municipal Public Works Bureau signed the loan contract with Asia Development, it began preparations. The bureau has submitted to the municipal government for approval to establish the South Shanghai Bus Management Office, with Zhang Dengyi, chief of the fourth section of the bureau, concurrently serving as director, and Jin Baoxian, director of the accounting section of the first section of the bureau, concurrently serving as deputy director. The office is also divided into three sections: technology, business, and general affairs, each with a section chief. The technology section is concurrently headed by Qin Zhihui, a technician of the bureau, the business section is concurrently headed by Deputy Director Jin, and the general affairs section is headed by Zhang Fufeng, chief of the general affairs section of the first section of the bureau. The organization has been established, and it can be operated on a selected date after the Asia Development Company delivers the buses. 142

The Shanghai-Hangzhou section branch office of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Workers' Union convened a temporary delegates' meeting at the Jiaxing office due to issues such as annual salary increases and passed 11 resolutions, requesting the two railways unions to make demands to the two railway bureaus and set a deadline of three days (last Saturday) for a reply. After receiving the news, the railway bureau selectively replied electrically to each station along the Shanghai-Hangzhou line, ignoring the workers' union. Therefore, the workers' union believed that the railway bureau's reply procedure was inappropriate. After convening a management meeting for three days, it reasoned with the railway bureau and extended the deadline to three days, requesting the bureau to reply. At that time, the situation was very serious. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency learned from the railway bureau's staff that, as of yesterday, Xiao Weiguo, director of the bureau's transportation department, had once gone to Hangzhou to convene a sectional affairs meeting to discuss the solution to the matter and convened Jiaxing branch office staff to explain in detail. It is learned that yesterday the railway bureau had replied to each request separately. The details of the process are recorded as follows.

Employee Requirements (1) Clearly announce the specific methods for determining annual salary increases and performance appraisals. Before the announcement, it should be handled according to the usual practice, and those who did not receive an annual salary increase in the first half of the 22nd year should be paid retroactively (including those who were reprimanded once, they should still receive the increase). (2) Relax the salary limit for laborers. (3) Station laborers should all be paid substitute holiday pay. (4) Transportation employees working on various commemorative holidays designated by the National Government should be given substitute holiday pay. (5) Annual salary increase for transportation employees for the second half of the 22nd year. (6) Employees should not be allowed to apply for leave retroactively after being sick. (7) The case of unfair punishment of transportation employees in the gatehouse car burning case. (8) Stationmaster Cao Zheshou's salary was reduced due to a demerit, and it has been more than a year and has not been restored to the original salary. "It is proposed that according to the usual practice, the original salary can be restored within six months after the punishment, if there is no fault." (9) Freight clerk Yao Dexin and stationmaster Shen Weibin were each reprimanded once, but they each received a commendation once during the "January 28th" incident, and did not receive an annual salary increase. (10) Train conductors Tao Yong and Zheng Guoliang have been promoted and should be given a salary increase according to precedent. (11) In October of the 21st year, train No. 408 did not exchange a road sign when passing Wangdian Station. After a year, Li Qifa was inexplicably reprimanded and his salary was reduced. 144

Railway Bureau Reply (1) It is agreed to actively cooperate in the evaluation and announce it. For the salary increase employees announced in the first half of the 22nd year, those who were warned will be refunded for the loss of delayed salary increase. (2) Station laborers will be allowed to be promoted to full-time road workers as much as possible. If they cannot qualify in the annual examination, they will be allowed to seek remedial measures. (3) Employees who do not have a regular holiday within a month will be paid one day's substitute holiday pay. (4) After confirming the various locations, it will be allowed to be handled in the same way. (5) The General Bureau has completed the review and will announce it soon. (6) Employees at outside stations who are sick and cannot go to the medical office for treatment can submit the sick treatment certificate to the medical officer for a sick leave within a week. If they are sick due to returning to their hometown from a long distance, they can submit the certificate to the road officer for a supplementary holiday. (7) The files will be re-examined and the handling methods will be determined separately. (8) It will be allowed to restore the original salary. (9) It will be announced after the examination committee reviews and determines it. (10) Submit it to the recent bureau affairs meeting for discussion and decision, and then announce it. (11) The entire case will be investigated and then replied to. 145

Labor Strife Subsides The branch office convened a committee meeting at the Jiaxing meeting site yesterday and resolved to accept the bureau's replies to various items and end the committee's mission. In the future, the management committee will continue to be responsible for handling matters. As for the employees, after the director of the road transportation department and Shen, the general section chief, and Chen Bohua, a director of the union, worked hard to explain, the situation has subsided. 146

Ministry of Communications Revises the Method of Postal Transfer of Telegrams Postage Waived 148

According to the Ministry of Communications' official telegram, starting from March 15th of this year, postage for postal transfer of telegrams should be waived. Starting from that date, each bureau should handle postal transfer of telegrams according to the following methods: (1) Charge according to the domestic telegram rates, postage is waived. (2) When handing over for postal delivery, the telegram should be placed in a visible-envelope postal transfer telecommunications envelope. If there is no such envelope, a regular telegram envelope may be used temporarily, stating the name and address of the recipient, and adding the postal affairs stamp and the name stamp of the handler. No postage stamps should be affixed. Use a telegram delivery book to clearly indicate the date, number, telegram type, number of words, and the place of dispatch and receipt, and submit it to the local post office or agency for inspection and receipt. Then, the postal stamp should be affixed in the telegram delivery book, and no receipt should be given. Seal the envelope and deliver it to the recipient. The above-mentioned (postal affairs) stamp should be carved locally by each bureau. It is a wooden stamp 1.2 inches long and 0.8 inches wide (standard size). The telegram delivery book will be printed and issued separately in this port. The ordinary delivery book will be used temporarily. In addition to separately telegraphing the Postal Administration to instruct each post office and agency to comply, each should comply.

Reaction to the Increased Commission in the Wuxi-Changzhou Grain Industry The commission for selling grain in Wuxi and Changzhou was generally converted at a 1% discount, which was the same as in Shanghai. After the lunar new year, the grain industry in Wuxi suddenly united with their counterparts in Changzhou, citing the rising cost of living, and changed to a 1.6% discount. Farmers and merchants in the northern Anhui production areas believed that grain prices had fallen to an extreme point, and they were on the verge of bankruptcy. The further increase in commission by Wuxi and Changzhou was unbearable. They jointly elected representatives Sun Yuanfu, Li Peisheng, and Hu Hanqing to go south for negotiations and submitted a petition to the competent authorities. It is heard that the result of the petition was satisfactory. At a time when the sound of economic depression is filling the air and farmers and merchants across the country are in distress, the sudden increase in commission by the Wuxi and Changzhou grain industries is contrary to the government's purpose of rescuing rural areas. Its impact is by no means insignificant. Moreover, the level of cost of living is undoubtedly higher in Shanghai, but the grain industry in Shanghai has not increased, so it is no wonder that the farmers and merchants in the production areas are firmly opposed. The representatives arrived in Shanghai today and are expected to hold negotiations. 150

Invention of Instant Photography: A Great Contribution to the Printing, Plate-making, and Photography Industries. Since the invention of photography to this day, there have been over a hundred years. The speed of progress and the breadth of application have long been recognized by the world. However, today, apart from the significant improvements in quality and efficiency compared to the past, the methods used are essentially the same as before. Scholars continue to use old methods, regarding them as the only way in photography, almost forgetting their shortcomings and disregarding costs, which is truly regrettable. Our renowned photography scholar, Professor Gao Weixiang, has long been aware of this. During his time studying in Europe, he dedicated himself to researching reform methods. After several years and numerous setbacks, he recently announced the success of his experimental research, inventing the so-called "Instant Photography," which has the following characteristics: (1) No need to purchase dry plates or films; (2) Direct capture of positive and negative images as media for ink printing and photosensitive printing; (3) Light sensitivity and color reproduction are superior to today's fastest and best dry plates or films; (4) From shooting to printing photos or making printing molds, it only takes a quarter of an hour; (5) The richness and fidelity of the obtained tones are unmatched by any printing paper or copying method; (6) No need for photosensitive paper, developing, fixing, and other procedures for copying. Its simplicity and economy are the same as monochrome or multicolor printing; (7) All intermediate steps of ordinary copying, plate-making, and reprinting are eliminated, greatly increasing printing efficiency; (8) No need to use lead type for printing books and newspapers. All typesetting and illustrations are completely replaced by photosensitive automatic methods; (9) All methods of using photography for recording, transmission, and copying, such as plate-making, photocopying, telephoto transmission, military photography, etc., will be exceptionally fast; (10) Dry and wet plates with weak light sensitivity can also be used for the shortest instant photography. This invention is one of the greatest contributions to the printing, plate-making, and photography industries in recent times. Its impact will surely revolutionize the old methods that have been used before. Mr. Gao is young and handsome, having studied in Europe for many years, specializing in photochemistry and colloid chemistry. He graduated from the Chemistry Department and the Photography Department of the German National University of Technology. He is very interested in research and writing, so his great invention is by no means accidental. It is heard that Mr. Gao has recently obtained the priority to apply for patents in various countries and is currently in contact with a large foreign manufacturer regarding production matters, hoping to produce it as soon as possible. It is also heard that Mr. Gao has compiled his invention's principles, methods, and applications into a long paper, entrusting it to be published by the "Photographic Journal" of the Royal Photographic Society of Great Britain and the German Photographic Communication Magazine published by the Austrian National Film Academy to promote public attention. Mr. Gao is now preparing everything and plans to hold a public experimental lecture at a famous academic institution in this city in the near future, which will surely attract the attention of the Chinese people.

Dockworkers Clash at Sino-American Wharf: Court Holds Preliminary Hearing Yesterday. The Sino-American Petroleum Company's newly built wharf at Dinghai Road contracted all loading and unloading matters to Rongji Company. However, since Rongji started work last month, more than two hundred people claiming to be dockworkers have come forward to prevent work from proceeding. Sino-American Company petitioned the Municipal Public Security Bureau for protection. On the 26th of last month, Director Wen Hongen ordered the captain of the Third Squadron of the Police Brigade, Pei Chengzhu, along with squad leader Fu Jichuan and more than ten officers, to station themselves there. Unexpectedly, on the following day (the 27th), more than two hundred people suddenly came during Rongji's work, each carrying iron rulers and wooden sticks, severely injuring squad leader Fu and two police officers. Three people on their side were also seriously injured and sent to Sacred Heart Hospital on nearby Ningguo Road for treatment. On the second day, Captain Pei arrested Han Dexin, a Shandong man who was leading the group, at Yangshupu Little Vegetable Market and sent him to the First Special Court to be handed over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation and detention. Unexpectedly, among the more than two hundred people, Pan Zhenggang, Xu Binggen, and others recently filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai Local Court against Li Xiahong, the manager of Rongji Company, for inflicting injuries. Yesterday, both parties were summoned to the court for a preliminary hearing. Rongji sent representative Qiu Xin to the court to state the course of events. According to Qiu's testimony in court, Rongji Company contracts the work of transporting goods to more than twenty wharves and factories. Manager Li Xiahong is only responsible for compensation for lost items of cargo owners. The work in various places is handled by dedicated personnel in each place. Zhang Qingshan is responsible for the loading and unloading matters at the Sino-American Petroleum Wharf. Finally, Qiu requested the court to investigate in detail whether the plaintiffs were genuine dockworkers, otherwise, there may be other purposes. After the interrogation, the court ordered a rescheduling for further interrogation.

"Bulito" Trademark Dispute Resolved. The "Bulito" produced by Jiufu Pharmaceutical Company in this city is effective in treating lung diseases and coughs, being the only domestically produced medicine for the symptoms. Since its launch, it has become popular far and wide. However, due to the dispute with the American Pader Company's "Pareto" trademark in terms of pronunciation, the two parties have been in litigation for many years. Until recently, after the interpretation by the Judicial Yuan and the decision by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the dispute of Pader Pharmaceutical Company was clearly unfounded. Therefore, the legally created "Bulito" trademark of Jiufu Company can finally stand tall under the blue sky and white sun, fulfilling its important mission of improving national health. This year, to expand its effectiveness, three new types have been added: "Arsenic-containing," "Iodine-containing," and "Regulation-containing," along with the existing "Pure" and "Quiguai-containing" types, totaling five types, each with its own characteristics, each playing its great role according to its suitable symptoms. They are now ready for distribution and will be launched soon. The existing "Pure" and "Quiguai-containing" Bulito are available for sale in major pharmacies and companies in various cities that sell new medicines. It is advisable to take Bulito for those with weakened bodies in the spring and suffering from colds and coughs. You can purchase it on the market.

Two Straw Boats Burned. Two straw boats were moored at the foot of the new garbage bridge on Xizang Road. Yesterday afternoon at 1:07 p.m., someone threw a cigarette butt onto the boat. Before long, thick smoke filled the air, and flames shot out in all directions. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to rescue the boats, but due to the piercing northerly wind and the easy ignition of the straw, it took more than two hours to extinguish the fire. As a result, both boats were reduced to ashes, with only the hulls remaining, sinking into the Suzhou River.

However, Hebei has produced heroes throughout history, and it is said in history that "Yan and Zhao have many generous and tragic figures," such as Jing Ke assassinating the King of Qin, and the song of farewell at the Yi River, "The wind is rustling, the Yi River is cold; once a hero departs, he will never return." How tragic and generous! Regardless of the success or failure of this act, the great integrity of dedicating oneself to the country is truly admirable to future generations (the following is omitted). After the group photo, entertainment began, such as the drum performance at the Tianchan Bookstore, the motorcycle stunts at the Great World, the Shanghai Opera and Peking Opera at the Yayun Society and Juyou Society, the martial arts troupe, and Yang Lianqin's iron sheet drum performance, which were all very popular for a time. The meeting adjourned at 10 p.m.

Reading and Answering Questions About the Exploration of Tariff Autonomy (I). Reading Guidance: Recently, I have been studying the issue of tariffs and have read some books. I have strong doubts about some of the claims made. I am now writing down my doubts and personal opinions to ask you about them. To save valuable space, I will not add many references, and I will not mention book titles or names. Most Chinese scholars, not just scholars, but also political parties, have always had the problem of blindly adhering to established methods. For example, regarding the "issue of China's tariff autonomy," as far as I know today, it is no longer a legal issue but a factual issue. Because China's tariffs have legally been conceded by the powers, and it has the right to autonomy. China today is about to increase tariffs by 200 percent, which is also legally based. As for the reason why China cannot implement tariff protection policies like other countries, according to my consideration, it is because China's national industry has, in fact, formed an organic link with the economic aggression of imperialism, including finance and goods. For example, silk factories and rayon, yarn factories and flour mills and foreign cotton and wheat, are the most prominent examples. Therefore, the legal acquisition of this tariff autonomy is only nominal. From this, we can know that the tariff issue in China today is no longer a simple external demand for autonomy, but an internal demand for implementing protective tariffs. However, these scholars and political parties who are blind and adhere to established methods still publish their demands for China's tariff autonomy in their articles and list them in their political programs. Is this their mistake of waiting for rabbits to bump into trees, or do they have other reasons for saying so? My limited knowledge is really unable to fathom their profoundness. Please take the time to enlighten me! However, there is one point I want to state clearly. If their basis is that China has most-favored-nation treaty relationships with the major imperialist countries, it cannot unilaterally impose high tariffs on a certain type of goods from a certain country. When it comes to universal implementation, it is hindered by the financial and industrial relations between some countries' similar goods being imported and our country's current rulers, so even though there is the nominal tariff autonomy, it still cannot escape the reality of the "open door." Therefore, it is considered that China's external war still needs to purely demand tariff autonomy. However, I believe that this only indicates: (1) that our country's lack of autonomy is known to the powers; (2) that the powers are afraid that China will become a vassal of one country, so there is this restriction; (3) therefore, the core of the problem still lies in our country's lack of pursuit of autonomy, not in others not allowing our country to have autonomy. Although their permission for our country in this regard may be because they have recognized that our country cannot be autonomous, so they are doing this superficial favor? However, after they have played this set of tricks on the tariff issue, the focus of the problem has really changed. It has changed the refusal of autonomy into the inability of autonomy. Therefore, I believe that if we use these facts as the basis for the tariff still needing to purely demand external autonomy, I do not agree with this. This is foolish. We must know that imperialism is smart, and it has clearly shown that we have the responsibility to destroy China's economic independence, and Chinese national capitalists who are fully compradoristic also have a relationship. How can we turn a blind eye? Of course, we cannot therefore relax our vigilance against imperialism. Please correct whether these views are correct or not. (Qin Jing's letter)

Spring Changes. Xianxian. In recent years, the changes in the cheongsam can hardly be described as "rapid," but high collars, low collars, square collars, round collars, stiff collars, soft collars, just the collar alone are enough to say that there is a small change every three days and a major change every five days. The rest, such as the placket, sleeves, piping, and slits, are constantly changing. Unless you open your eyes wide and follow the trend of change step by step, you will inevitably fall behind. Because of the changes in women's cheongsams, I feel that it is really not easy to be a person in this era, because our environment is also constantly changing like the style of cheongsam. In order to adapt to the environment and sacrifice individuality, but when the successfully transformed individuality adapts to the environment, the environment has changed very subtly again. After watching, just as you will grasp the times, the times cruelly turn their heads and leave you behind. Education is also the same. University system and specialized system, three-three system and two-four system, preparatory system and high school system, academic year system and credit system. A certain system, imported from the East and West for less than a year, and before the trial is effective, the second academic system has already been imported, and its theory is better than the first. Naturally, unwilling to fall behind, we have to try the second one, but just as we start, the better third one is waving to you there. Therefore, human customs are also changing non-stop. From emphasizing chastity and building arches, to advocating freedom of marriage, widows should not observe chastity, and then transforming to abandoned wives and widows without status in society, it is not easy to find a partner, because abandoned wives and widows are no longer virgins. Smoking opium used to be a grand scene, and then everyone thought that smoking opium was a vulgar activity, a decadent act, but recently, without putting on a show, taking a few puffs of opium does not count as a high-class Chinese person. The marriage issue has changed from the orders of parents and the words of matchmakers to free combination, and then from free combination to "with the consent of both parents after being introduced by Mr. XX," and recently it has changed to "what about the two of us?" Look, European countries are also changing there. From autocracy to democracy to dictatorship. This set of tricks is really variable.

Northeast Four Company Commanders. Zhang Henshui. Chapter Twenty-Fifth. Tearful faces send people away from home to return to the distant garrison. The wind and sand are clear all night, and the fortress is stationed alone. Zhao Ziqiang said, "Since the battalion commander has a telegram to go, how can I not come? Not to mention that I have been married for several days, even if it was the first day of my marriage, and the order arrived the next day, I would still have to come." Baofang stretched out her thumb and smiled, saying, "Good. Soldiers must be like this, from the ordinary soldier to the commander-in-chief, they are all heroes, and China will be strong." The regimental commander told me to send you a telegram, so I sent you a telegram according to his instructions. As for why, I don't know either. Two days ago, enemy planes flew over the Great Wall, and the atmosphere was a bit tense. I haven't heard any news these past two days, so it seems to have calmed down again." On the way, Ziqiang kept thinking that maybe there was some change on the front line. When he arrived at the regimental headquarters, he didn't see any special activity, so he thought it was odd. At first, he thought it was a military secret, so it hadn't been announced yet. Now, the battalion commander also said that nothing was happening, so the regimental commander hadn't revealed anything either. Even if something was happening, it wasn't that urgent. He regretted why he hadn't stayed at home for a few more days. Baofang was talking, and saw that Ziqiang's attitude was slowly changing, and he seemed a bit hesitant, so she smiled and said, "You must think that I sent this telegram too early. Even if you stayed at home for two more days, nothing would have happened." Ziqiang blushed and forced a smile, saying, "I don't think so. Even if I stayed at home for two more days, I would have to leave home at this time anyway. What's the difference between arriving two days late and arriving two days early?" Baofang smiled and said, "Of course there's a difference. You go rest for a while, and I'll go tell the regimental commander that you've arrived." Ziqiang saw that the battalion commander had nothing to say, so he returned to his company headquarters. At this time, the sound of the wind howling in the sky was even more intense, and sometimes it suddenly increased in force, rolling up the sand and small pieces of wood on the ground, making a rustling sound on the roof. Ziqiang sat in a small room, supporting his head with both hands, thinking deeply. (330)

On the contrary, beauty-loving friends prepare their own safety razors and shave their beards in front of the mirror every day. Every ten or twenty days, they go to the beauty salon to sit for two hours. Not only do they not have the distress of "necessity," but they also think it is "pleasant," a required course for social interaction. Because everyone, regardless of old or young, men or women, and even bald people, has the opportunity to approach the barber. Taking advantage of sitting on a spring seat and draped in a snow-white scarf, thinking about the various things about the barber during the most leisurely one or two hours is also a very interesting pastime. The barber's uniform is white as the standard, just like the nurses in the hospital. But I think it might as well prepare a few more colors, such as the stimulating red, the feudal tiger yellow, the bright tender green, and the elegant violet, so that customers can have the pleasure of refreshing and pleasing the eye. The barber's work has three major procedures: first, trimming; second, neatening; third, combing. It symbolizes the improvement of national affairs. Barbers also pay special attention to the art of beauty, which is a free procedure that is mutually related to their profession, just like a person who can do things, can eat, and also wants fame. Barbers can also perm hair, perming it into exquisite art patterns. Although the profession is small, it is worth respecting as an "artist." Barbers have the ability to organize hair that is as messy as a hedgehog into a well-organized and orderly manner, whether your hair has always been leaning to the left or to the right. After his kindness and power are applied together, stroking and combing, the rebellious will be corrected root by root. This wonderful skill is worthy of public admiration! Commercial News, Finance, Gold Market Sharpness

Exchange Rate Extremely Tight, Hedging Activity

Continued to Rise by Four Yuan and Five Jiao

Yesterday, the gold market saw the exchange rate become tight, leading to long-dormant hedging activity suddenly becoming active. Banks had a very healthy appetite, and large players were very eager to hedge in, with strong short covering as well, resulting in a sharp market situation in the first half of the day, with a firm trend. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw London contract and the US remain flat. The forward silver price on the Five Metals Exchange rose by varying amounts, from seven hao to two li and a half. Exchange rate fluctuations were minimal. London raw gold rose by four pence, US cotton fell by nine points, US wheat contracted by half a point. The wool market opened slightly lower, falling to around 47 yuan. Soon after, large players such as Fuchang and Qianchangxiang entered the market together, and the situation gradually rose. After opening, the exchange rate became tight, and there were rumors that India was selling silver. Large players such as Hengyu, Zhifeng, Yongrun, Changyu, Dadecheng, Tianfeng, and Yong etc. advanced aggressively, with Chengfeng and Yong covering shorts. Although Bingxing and Guangbang, etc., supplied the market, the domestic market continued to tighten, and banks showed a strong appetite. Hedging activity among peers gradually increased, and the situation was strongest at noon. After closing, the price rose even further to over 55 yuan.
