Private banks to regularly open an afternoon market for transactions

Starting March 10 ### 155

The money market has traditionally opened two sessions daily, morning and afternoon, for trading. Since February 18, due to the Lunar New Year holiday, all industries were quiet, and public business and goods were not moving, demand for funds was light. Therefore, the money industry also followed customs, stopping trading, and only opening the morning session for trading. Currently, commerce is gradually prospering, and the circulation of various aspects is also increasing. Procedures are more tedious and cumbersome. Therefore, the Market Committee decided to reopen the afternoon session for trading on March 10 (Saturday). In this way, two sessions will still be opened daily thereafter, without interruption, restoring its former appearance. Stock bonds hover and brew a rising trend

Yesterday, the market situation in the Chinese Stock Exchange, generally observed, was still hovering and brewing, but the trend was already strong, and it may still go uphill first, then downhill. Generally, most people think that bulls will certainly not easily leave, and bears are also unwilling to cover immediately. New bulls are also tasteless, and try very little, so they tend to hover. Few know that in these days, the hovering has aroused the interest of short sellers, and the accumulated transactions, although small, are not few in number. A slight replenishment can easily raise the price. Judging from the environment, there is also no reason for a sudden drop, and it cannot always hover and brew like this. Based on the above summary, there is an observation that we will see a high side first. Judging from the price trend of the upper and lower afternoon markets yesterday, and the situation of adoption or abandonment by various gangs, there is also no sign of a quick downturn. Transactions in No. 4, 12, and 35 were in greater demand. The sellers were still sporadic retail investors, and they were more enthusiastic. Although the rises and falls of each market were small, in general, the overall trend rose throughout the day. In fact, the buyers were unwilling to raise prices, and the sellers firmly demanded higher prices. A rough look seems to be still hovering, but it already has a tendency to rise secretly. If we see new high prices again, there should still be about one yuan of good prospects. The market price results uniformly rose by one jiao to four jiao. The 22 Customs was the only one to rise by nine jiao because No. 46 had already stopped being sold, so it still felt cheaper than other types. The total number of transactions was 5,496,000 yuan, including 1,000 yuan in spot goods and 5,495,000 yuan in futures. Grain and flour futures market saw Tianjin gangs selling out in the morning

Yesterday's flour market, after the market opened in the morning, the market for each month turned weak again. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat was about 2 jiao lower in Chicago and 1 jiao lower in Canada, the market was flat and tired after opening. In addition, the saying that large factories would stop production had not yet been implemented, and the sales of customer gangs were still not strong. Therefore, Tianjin gangs had sold out, so the market for each month entered a soft road again. When the market opened in the afternoon, the market for each month tended to hover, because the factory's chips had not been issued, and the minds of outsiders were still stable, so there was little entry and exit. The future rise depends on the foreign market changing. As a result, this month fell by 1 fen, April and May fell by 1 fen, June fell by 1 fen 7 li and a half, July and August fell by 1 fen and a half.

Because there were no new chips added to the buying and selling, the market speculation had no way to start. Nantong: Police Officer Shelters Opium Trafficker Case 156

Hu Jinlong, a police officer from the Yaogang Public Security Bureau, sheltered opium trafficker Yang Guoxiang. After investigation by the county government, Hu and Yang were both sent to the court for interrogation. Chief Prosecutor Liu Shizhu opened the court for investigation. Yang Guoxiang confessed that he gave Hu Jinlong kickbacks on a monthly basis. The court ordered Yang Guoxiang to be detained, and Hu Jinlong to be held in custody by the Nantong County Public Security Bureau.

Jiaxing: Further Inquiry into Police Causing Trouble 157

Qian Wenbin, the police chief of the Tianning Temple police station in Jiaxing, took nude pictures from the Shenghe Grocery Store on Beida Street, which aroused dissatisfaction among the onlookers and led to a quarrel. Subsequently, the police officers of the police station went out armed and beat people, causing the police whistle to sound in chaos. The fire brigades of various neighborhoods mistakenly thought it was a fire and arrived at the scene one after another. Afterwards, some of the public and reporters gathered in front of the county public security bureau, and were shot at by the police, causing injuries to Shen Jinguan and others. The details have been recorded in the newspaper on the 6th. Now, Shen Jinguan has died of serious injuries, and because his family has nothing, the county chamber of commerce has temporarily advanced 200 yuan for funeral expenses. At the same time, the father of the deceased, Shen Jiqing, appealed to the county party headquarters and various legal groups to organize a support association. Prosecutor Wang Bangyan of the local court has successively inspected the injured and the deceased at Dexin and Jiaxing hospitals, and also went to the Public Security Bureau and the police station to survey the overturned objects. The police chief Qian Wenbin who caused the incident has been sent to the court detention center to prepare for interrogation. The general public still hopes that Director Gao will investigate the police officers who fired the shots and send them to court for interrogation. It is also learned that after the provincial department received reports from both sides on the cause of the incident, it will send personnel to He to investigate. The county party headquarters has issued a notice to all county residents, ordering them to strictly maintain order and wait for a resolution. On the morning of the 7th, it convened a meeting of representatives from the county chamber of commerce, the fire brigade, the first district office, and the county government to discuss the punishment of the police chief who caused the incident and the compensation for the injured and dead. The resolution was: (1) To form a tragedy committee, organized by various legal groups and local gentry. The county chamber of commerce will be designated to draft an organizational outline and be responsible for convening its establishment. The outline will be submitted to the county party headquarters for record. (2) The county party headquarters will send a letter to the directors of various legal groups to jointly investigate all the details of the case impartially with the party and government, and create a fair report to be sent to the administrative and judicial organs as powerful evidence. (3) The county party headquarters and the county chamber of commerce will separately raise funds to compensate the family members of the deceased Shen Jinguan and subsidize the medical expenses of the injured.

Jiashan: Farmers Gather to Beat and Injure Tax Collectors 158

In Luosi Canal area, Beixiang Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, farmer Hu Youfa has cultivated three or four hundred acres of farmland and is quite wealthy. The other day was his birthday, and he held a banquet. It happened that Wang Jinmin, a tax collector for the third district's land tax, came to Hu's place to collect taxes. A fight broke out due to words. Hu Youfa's son and brother surrounded and beat Wang Jinmin, causing him to be seriously injured all over his body. On the spot, dozens of yuan of collected donations were also lost. For a time, the public was very angry. Such rudeness can endanger the lives of civil servants everywhere. In addition to reporting to the district office for handling, Wang Jinmin also filed a criminal lawsuit with the court in person.

Seven-Year-Old Child Kidnapped and Case Cracked 159

Jin Youhao, a farmer in the area bordering Jiaxing County outside the west gate of this county, is quite wealthy. He has a child who is only seven years old and attends a nearby elementary school. Suddenly, in the middle of the night the other day, more than a dozen bandits broke down the door and entered, forbidding anyone from making a sound. After looting, they kidnapped the seven-year-old child and left. Jin Youhao reported to the Weidi (禾地, a name for Jiaxing) and the local county security group for strict investigation. Soon, the child's whereabouts were discovered near Xinmou Town under the jurisdiction of Jiaxing. The security group sent a team to follow and arrested many male and female kidnappers and four boy and girl hostages according to the address. They were all sent to this county. After County Chief Yang interrogated them, he immediately imprisoned them.

Yixing: Establishment of Jiangsu Farmers Bank Branch is Scheduled 160

Since the establishment of the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank, its business has been expanding day by day. Currently, there are already 23 branches and business offices scattered throughout the province. The counties where branches have not yet been established are requesting their establishment one after another. The Yixing County Agricultural Bank's funds have recently reached a considerable amount, and the request to establish a branch has been approved by General Manager Zhao of the Agricultural Bank. Deputy Manager Hou Houpei of the bank personally went to the county to investigate in detail and look for a new branch location. He has now returned to the province after completing his official duties. It is reported that the impression of this investigation is quite good. Once the branch building is found, it can be established in the near future.

American Aviator Hawkes Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 161

Today, he will take a giant bomber to Hangzhou for assembly.

After assembly in two or three weeks, he will fly the plane to Shanghai for a performance.

The plane can carry 30 people and 4,000 pounds of bombs.

Major Hawkes, a famous American aviator, was invited by Mr. Pauley, the China representative of the Curtis-Wright Airplane Company, to bring his wife and pilot Galls and the giant bomber Condor to China for a performance. He arrived in Shanghai on the President McKinley, a steamer of the Dollar Steamship Lines, at 8:30 yesterday morning. He is scheduled to take the plane to Hangzhou for assembly today, and will perform in Shanghai in two or three weeks. The details are as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 162

At about 7:00 yesterday morning, it arrived at the Balianjing Wharf in Pudong. Mr. Hawkes and others transferred to a ferry and landed at the New Customs Wharf at 8:30, and stayed at the Cathay Hotel.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Commentary

Sports Litigation 168

— Chen

At the Second National Games, it was heard that several world records were broken. At a time when our country cannot compete on the world's political and economic stage, it must be said that it is a great honor for this weak nation. Therefore, our patriotic people have found a great way to save the country and revitalize the nation from this fact, and shouted, "Save the country through sports." The meaning is that the prosperity of the country and nation depends on healthy citizens, and healthy citizens rely on strong bodies, and strong bodies depend on promoting sports and developing exercise. Their sincere patriotic intentions are reasonable and justified.

However, in this "national salvation avenue," there are many "deeply distressing" facts. According to reports, on December 16 last year, Jiaotong University and Jinan University held a Jiangnan University football match, and Shen Huichun, a member of the China Sports Referee Association, was hired as a notary. Because Jiaotong University lost, they vented their anger on the referee. Students such as Qin Shaoji actually beat Shen Huichun seriously injured. Both sides were unwilling to back down, and filed a lawsuit with the local court. As a dignified national university, they actually went to court for this "competition" dispute, no wonder "public opinion was in an uproar." This issue aroused the mediation of Mr. Wang Zhengting, the chairman of the National Sports Association, and evolved into the "Shen Case" in the history of the sports world, which is also a "nationally watched" shocking event.

If we observe this issue with the perspective of "saving the country through sports," how did it arise, and what is its impact on society? We cannot help but say a few words here. If the purpose of sports is to strengthen the people or even to promote "national salvation," then it should never be about raising a few athletes and "trophy" collectors, but should expand the scope of the people and carry out a wide range of popularization work. Because the ultimate goal of sports is always to temper the body, and it is never for the sake of sports, or for the sake of trophies and silver medals.

However, this true meaning has not been understood. The fact that sports have become a "circle" and sports have become "experts" has already explained this. Although there are many sports organizations, "clubs," and "teams" in various circles, generally speaking, sports are a patent of students and intellectuals. In particular, many school authorities regard trophies and silver shields as advertisements to attract students, and cultivate athletes with the same enthusiasm as dog track owners. This is an undeniable fact. Under this trend, two morbid states are created: on the one hand, the "aristocratization" of sports, and on the other hand, the vanity of experts who take sports as a profession and a place to settle down. The virtue of the first fact can be seen in many school athletes who do not attend classes, do not repeat grades, drink milk, and receive subsidies; and the manifestation of the second phenomenon is the many "fans" and the "cheerleading squads" of female students in various schools. Therefore, under the mutual use of cultivation and vanity, many indecent situations have arisen in the Chinese sports world, and the so-called "Shen Case" is only a small part of it.

It is said that this "Shen Case," which shocked the sports world, has been resolved through the mediation of Mr. Wang Zhengting, relying on the power of this "interpreter," but the pathological phenomenon of sports bias remains the same. Whenever we spend five cents or one yuan to come out of the YMCA Central Sports Field, as if we have entered a dog track or rabbit track once, and think of many people who are weak and isolated from sports, who have no place and no possibility to exercise, we always feel infinitely "deeply distressed" about the future of this "sports saving the country."

Page 20

In the Teahouse 169

— Dai Ni

Random Notes on Returning Home

I ran out alone, but had nowhere to go. My hometown was so unfamiliar to me. I cast another nostalgic glance at the old trees and broken houses, and then walked aimlessly forward on the cobblestone path that seemed familiar.

Many people slipped past me, many houses slipped past me, I felt like I was dreaming. Is this my hometown? The question in front of me led me to the street.

The three words "Wangjianglou" (Overlooking the River Teahouse) came into my view. This was the place I used to rest every day. I don't like tea, but I used to use it to relieve boredom; now it has become a habit. At that time, it seemed like someone was urging me to step inside. The person in charge of the tea stove was surprised: "Young Master XX is back?" He stared at me as I sat down at the teatable. Doesn't he dream? I thought:

Wangjianglou is a three-story building built on the only official road in my hometown, and it is called "Overlooking the River" for that reason. There are regular tea drinkers who come every day, rain or shine, and have fixed seats (I used to be one of them). In the past five years, the teahouse has probably changed, and many people are no longer familiar to me. Several people nodded to me because the tea server said "Young Master XX," or asked awkwardly, "Back from Shanghai?" I no longer belong to my hometown, my hometown has forgotten me!

Those newly emerging tea drinkers are no different from the past. They talk about rice prices every day. The bankruptcy of the countryside has nothing to do with them. They are all big landlords. Now they are talking about the rice prices. Yesterday, someone surnamed XX sold hundreds of dan of rice for X yuan and X jiao, and today someone surnamed XX sold rice and the price has risen by two jiao. I seemed to hate their expressionless attitude, but wasn't I like this before? I have truly been abandoned by my hometown.

The old gentleman sitting in the corner, who used to be my chess partner, now opened his mouth: "I heard that the official road on the dam is going to be opened?"

This question gave everyone a stimulus. Damming the river and hoarding rice are conflicting topics, so there was a discussion that didn't get to the point; just then a tea drinker came in, and the topic turned to a gambling game at the home of a tea drinker last night; someone had good luck, and someone lost thousands of yuan, and they could even recite the details of a certain domino last night, vividly. I opened my eyes wide, as if I was a gambler last night too.

"Monk Kills His Wife!" Someone shouted. What the teahouse needs is this kind of news, so even the most basic teahouse has a copy of the Shih Pao (Eastern Times), let alone Wangjianglou!

A group of people surrounded the table with the newspaper, snatching to read it and reading it aloud. After everyone understood the plot, they began to discuss it, but without a chairman. Some compared it to similar cases in the past, some... before long they talked about women's menstruation, genitals, and old people and young people talking about the same things, always smiling. The old man who proposed damming the river forgot that he was hoarding thousands of dan of rice at home and would suffer losses because of it, and the gambler who lost money last night also forgot that the thousands of yuan he lost were all silver dollars.

I walked to the bathroom. I saw two large lines under the words "Pay Attention to Hygiene": "Please take a step further for urination." I looked down from the window, and the destination of the funnel was this official road overlooking the river. My hometown doesn't have flush toilets, and no one pours out the night soil early in the morning. Their only place to clean the toilets is this official road. As for dumping garbage in the river, it's even more a matter of course. So, no matter what, the "water" in the teahouse is taken from this river, and it is "paying attention to hygiene" to "take a step further" for "urination" into the funnel.

I returned to my seat, and didn't dare to pick up the teapot again. I felt strangely greasy and wanted to vomit. Over there, the proposal for "Monk Kills His Wife" had not yet been put to a vote, and inexplicably the second proposal "Tonight's Gambling Game" occurred again. This seemed easier to resolve. A gambling game would continue at the home of the tea drinker from last night.

Before I knew it, twilight had gathered from all directions, and an afternoon came to an end. Many questions were left behind as people went home, or perhaps they would never talk about these kinds of questions again. What they remembered was tonight's gambling game. The topics of conversation in the teahouse tomorrow could arise temporarily, so there was no need to prepare urgently tonight; and... what else? I didn't come to Wangjianglou the next day.

Amateur Mailbox

Flower Vase 170

Mr. Editor:

After this letter reaches your editorial department, I hope you

can reply to me within three days. These three days are such precious time! If this deadline passes, I will decide to walk my own path. How I long to be enlightened by you, sir!

The problem is this: I am a graduate of higher primary school, and now I am working as a "flower vase" in a certain office. (A painful phrase!) Among many "flower vases," I am quite favored by the manager. In fact, that beast in human form harbors malicious intentions towards me. In three months, I have been subjected to his lewd jokes four times, and I have cleverly escaped his traps each time. At the end of last year, I originally wanted to resign immediately to respect our female dignity, but when I thought about my parents, siblings, and younger siblings starving after I lost my job, I felt it was better to endure the humiliation. As long as I am clever and have an iron will, he cannot subdue me. What do I have to fear? Unexpectedly, this unpredictable human wickedness has attacked me beyond my expectations. Last Friday night, that thing insisted on inviting me and another colleague to talk, ostensibly to discuss official business, but not in the office. Instead, he opened a room in a hotel. We knew his intentions as soon as we stepped into the hotel. Naturally, it wasn't about official business, because there were no male or female colleagues from the office, only him and a servant. He prepared a lot of food and wine to entertain us. I was only filled with anger and defensiveness, and had no intention of engaging in any shady business with him. Unexpectedly, things became more and more outrageous. After …, another … arrived, … he… particularly close to us. He said a lot of pointless things. Later, the manager even tricked my female colleague into another room. That young master didn't come back either. At this time, only he and I were in the room. He planned to get me drunk with wine, but I firmly refused to drink, and we argued until twelve o'clock. I insisted on leaving, but he wouldn't let me. I shouted and cried. The waiter pretended not to notice. I knew he had paid money, and he had arranged everything. At this time, I was only prepared to fight him to the death. It was unsuccessful, so I changed to pleading and using money as a soft tactic. Sir, that's how we made a scene all night. I was never subdued.

Sir, in this "bright daylight" Shanghai, can you believe that such insults to professional women actually happen?

I returned home at dawn the next day. I cried all day. I originally wasn't going to work anymore, but my family didn't understand. Instead, they suspected that I had someone else in my heart. I had no choice but to endure humiliation and shame to work for my family. Unexpectedly, this beast deliberately spread dirty words, creating a foul atmosphere to trap me and make me submit. On the third day, as soon as I entered the office, I saw many colleagues, some were angry, some were sneering, and some even congratulated me. Heavens! I cried and went home before I even finished work.

After suffering this kind of humiliation, sir! I can't bear it anymore. I can't consider my parents, siblings, and younger siblings anymore. I have no way to go. What hope do I have? Isn't it the same for women everywhere? Why should I live and be trampled by others?

Sir! I have decided that I only have Ai Xia's path to take!

However, I feel that there is still a glimmer of hope, but I want to find a first path to struggle. (I'm not afraid of death.) Ai Xia's death has already caused criticism, saying that she didn't have enough understanding. Sir! My situation is not as good as Ai Xia's, and my abilities are not as good as Ai Xia's, but before I live or die, I still want someone to guide me. I don't want to bear the accusation of "not having enough understanding" in this world again. Sir! Is there really a path for us women to take? Name temporarily hidden, March 5th.

After reading the above letter, the editor couldn't help but tremble, and tears couldn't help but well up in my eyes. In a state of extreme anxiety, I hurriedly looked for the date of mailing. Fortunately, the date of this letter is the 5th, and it's only been two days since today. Now that I have this opportunity, the editor respectfully and sincerely wants to tell Miss So-and-so, and also ask the female compatriots in the female community and all kind people who care about women's issues!

Regarding Miss So-and-so's problem, it is indeed not a surprising thing in today's society. This is already an open secret, and it happens everywhere every day. Society considers it too ordinary and not worth a second glance. Thousands upon thousands of women have either accepted this kind of trampling in silence or committed suicide. After suicide, society doesn't necessarily cause any surprise, and it ends up with some boring tabloids creating rogue, sensational material. Therefore! In such a society, when Miss So-and-so cries out, "Is there really a path for us women to take?" it is not out of her weakness, but rather it shows the seriousness of today's women's issue. Miss So-and-so's problem is naturally not her personal problem, but a serious problem shared by all professional women.

We greatly admire Miss So-and-so's spirit of struggle. In such a cold and indifferent society, even if she has the idea of committing suicide, we cannot strictly blame her. We can only sympathize and only find opportunities to enlighten her and increase her understanding. There is nothing else to say. What's more, Miss So-and-so herself clearly asks to "find another path to struggle." As the editor writes this, I feel even more uneasy. Looking at the alarming suicide news printed in today's newspapers every day, I think most of them are people who still want to live, but can't find the first path to struggle. Because they don't have Miss So-and-so's ability or level of understanding, the result is death in this contradiction. The responsibility is certainly borne by society, but we who survive still lack guidance. I think that if society had good guidance, many promising young men and women could be saved from this large group of suicides and their lives could be used on a path of striving for a better cause.

The following is the reply to Miss So-and-so:

According to the usual explanation, since Miss So-and-so is unwilling to endure this kind of humiliation anymore, the best way is to resign. The next best thing is to give that manager a serious warning, telling him that if he has any inappropriate behavior in the future, she will definitely take legal action. However, Miss So-and-so already knows that the first method is unsuccessful. She cannot watch her family "starve to death." As for the warning, it's even more of a joke, because since you still have to work under him now, how dare you offend him again? You certainly cherish your reputation and your body, but "eating is something that must also be taken into consideration!"

So the crux of the problem is: Under the chains of economic bondage, it is not surprising that women are insulted. This is bound to happen in a society where people use economic power to oppress others. Therefore, if Miss So-and-so really wants to seek liberation, it is not to resign and find another job, because "it is the same for women everywhere;" but to concentrate all her efforts on transforming society. This is by no means a lofty ideal, nor is it a distant path! It's a roundabout path. Because in this society, the pain that everyone feels cannot be solved by individual effort alone. There is a solution only after the fundamental transformation of society.

This is certainly a distant path, but what other path is there for us miserable people to take! And as long as we walk the path, no matter how far away it is, we will eventually reach it.

Novel

Lulu's Victory (Part 5) 172

— Written by Italian M. Serao, Translated by Jingxin

"My father is satisfied, my aunts all sent their congratulations, my cousins are angry, my friends congratulated me sarcastically in the coffee shop, my good friends shook my hand; so my marriage is very reasonable. I cannot deny that Lulu is very beautiful; when her eyes are so full of playfulness looking at me, when she laughs loudly showing her white teeth, I want to hold her little head in my hands and kiss her over and over again. Her attitude is elegant, her personality is lively, always cheerful and kind, always telling jokes and witty, always mischievous, never depressed, we can definitely get along well. I hate that kind of stern face, especially for the one I love. I seem to feel that in that kind of face, there is a secret sorrow hidden, I have not experienced this sorrow, and I don't know how to deal with it, or maybe this sorrow is caused by me. Sophia - my fiancée's sister, has this ability to bother me with her cold, unresponsive face. Every time I see her, my wisdom is useless, the smile leaves my lips; even if the most beautiful spring sun is shining, I seem to be banished to the gray November sky, even with Lulu I don't have the courage to joke; that Miss Sophia drives away all the joy. She may have seen the unpleasant impression she gives me, because she doesn't look at me when she talks to me, doesn't shake hands with me, and answers my questions with the simplest words. She must know that I don't like her. Maybe she is angry because of this.

"Lulu is always laughing loudly. She is very young. She has never said a serious word to me, even when she wants to be serious, it seems like she is joking. She loves me, but not to the point of frenzy. Frankly speaking, my love is not frenzied either; that's the best way. On my part, I have established two principles in my heart: first, engaged lovers should get along well; second, they should never start with a violent passion. Our situation is like this, so Lulu and I should be very happy. We will travel all over Italy, but not in a hurry, taking short trips, enjoying ourselves in extreme comfort, stopping wherever we like, and looking at even the most meaningless things. We will spend three months in this way; no, that's not enough, we can plan for four months; it would make me very happy to keep Lulu away from Sophia's boredom for a considerable period of time. But, I ask, is it natural for that girl to be so solemn at her age? She must be twenty-three years old. She refuses to say it clearly herself. In fact, she has beautiful eyes and a … frame, if she wasn't so stern-faced, she could be pleasant. I bet she will become an old maid; maybe that's her secret pain, maybe she has experienced love, an unfortunate love? -- I am very curious to know the reason for her stern face --, when Lulu and I are alone, I want to ask her --"

Film Special

Are American Film Publications Just Publicity Tools for Companies or Stars? 173

— Mi Qi

(1) The "Yes" Side (Part 1)

There are a total of twenty-two types of American film publications, referring to magazines. Their sales range from a minimum of 126,000 to a maximum of 565,000. I must know that the sales of American newspapers and magazines are almost all verified by a sales audit association and cannot be falsely reported. Therefore, the sales of more than twenty film magazines, taken together, form an important part of American social life and are also a facet of American culture. Statistically, a total of 8.8 million people spend ten or twenty cents each month to buy film magazines to read. If we take the average of two or three people reading one film magazine, which is still the lowest statistic, we can know that there are always two to three million people reading film magazines each month. And their influence is also very considerable.

Now some people say that these film magazines are loyal servants of Hollywood, hired propagandists, and tools of the stars. They cover up the countless sins in the film city and fan the flames of the sexually charged film industry, wielding influence in American society. The Hollywood film life and the status of the stars are depicted as magnificent and unapproachable, and their sole function is to act as mouthpieces for film companies, promoting their sales.

The above is the opening shot of a general attack on film publications. To prove the validity of the above statement, they examined the content of these magazines. They found many untrue and incomplete things in these magazines. The first is hearsay gossip. They say that gossip has become the central component of film magazines. What the first magazine publishes is all as much nonsense as possible, and no one is willing to seek to publicize the true situation of Hollywood. According to what is published in film magazines, Hollywood is the only paradise in America, the paradise in the world. Almost every magazine has a nonsense gossip column. They all have their Walter Winchell (a famous Hollywood reporter). They are all-knowing and all-understanding people; they can drill into everyone's heart and everyone's home to spy on news, so that they already know a piece of news before even the gods know it. Isn't this too vague and absurd?

In addition to short pieces of nonsense gossip, there are also many long articles. Where do these long articles come from? Even if they are not written by film companies or movie stars and submitted to the magazine for publication, they must be published with the authorization of related parties. Their content is also very empty and has no substantive news. They are mostly based on a star's gossip. If a smart person tries to investigate, he can discover that every time a long article about a star's life is published, it is immediately followed by the release of a film, and the star being promoted is also the protagonist of that film. We need to know that the editorial departments of these film magazines are all in cahoots with the advertising departments. There is no distinction between them. So these articles are all nonsense for a film or a star. For the sake of their own income, they willingly allow themselves to be used by the company authorities to fool the general public. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Eskimo" 174

— Ling He

Eskimo | Grand Theater |

When we accidentally discovered this "Eskimo" in the midst of the lewd atmosphere of a series of romantic love dramas in American films, we should immediately praise the author W.S. Van Dyke. Needless to say, we should give this work a very high evaluation.

In order to make it easier for readers to understand, I will briefly introduce it here. In 1927, he filmed "White Shadow in the South Seas" in the South Seas. In 1929, he went deep into the heart of Africa to film "Trader Horn," which we will never forget. As for this film, it was made in the Arctic Ocean in 1933. Undoubtedly, this is a great work.

First of all, let's talk about the structure of the story, from which we can see a glimpse of the idea.

First of all, what we need to know is why he wanted to use the Arctic Ocean as the background? This is of course because the wonders of icebergs and snow can be used as a spectacle on the screen, but what we should pay attention to now is how he adopts the material and how he handles the subject matter. In the middle of this, we can recognize his worldview.

In addition to introducing the life and customs of the local natives, "Eskimo" also unfolds their simple and brave character. They live primitively, and they struggle with nature for survival. They live by hunting. When they have no winter food, they must risk hunting walruses or polar bears. They are a group of people outside the civilized world. They have no sharp weapons, not even a single needle. There are no wars or any grudges between them. They live peacefully and lovingly, and they do not understand all the cunning and hypocrisy of civilized people.

However, precisely because of this, they are regarded as ignorant barbarians by the imperialist white people. So the white people exchange a few boxes of needles or a bird gun for their countless extremely valuable animal skins, and arbitrarily rape their women. However, they can comfort themselves by accepting the wives and daughters of others, but they cannot allow their own wives and daughters to be forcibly raped by civilized people, so they resist and kill the so-called civilized people who are beasts in human form. They do not understand the law, and they do not know what punishment they should receive. When Mala was captured by the civilized people after being deceived, he realized that the white people he had saved were now the executioners who would put him to death. For the sake of freedom and peace, they finally broke free from the shackles of imperialism. The harm they suffered from the white people was to escape in the snow and ice. They would not use the weapons of civilized people to hunt wild animals, so in hunger they had to kill their family dogs to satisfy their hunger.

Ah! Here, the cunning, hypocrisy, cruelty, and even the true face of all imperialism are exposed. The "Eskimo" people, who are considered savage, must not only work hard to fight against nature, but also escape the harm of so-called civilized people. Here, we are immediately reminded of Pudovkin's "Storm Over Asia." The primitive Mongols were deceived, abused, oppressed, and even inhumanly massacred by imperialists. In the end, the primitive Mongols finally rose up, finally exposed the true face of imperialism, and launched an anti-imperialist war. Similarly, the author of this "Eskimo" did not have a further understanding. All that Van Dyke could do was to describe the lovely life and personality of this primitive group of people with true sympathy. He only knew that they should resist for love, he only satirized the imperialists from the side, and he warmly sympathized with the fate of the barbarians. Until Mala was driven to escape on the melting ice floes, he made the young white man discover his conscience and not put him to death.

As mentioned above, we certainly cannot find a director in America like Pudovkin, but having this film is not necessarily a precious treasure among American films. After watching it, in the dialogue, he cursed the so-called civilized people, and he frankly taught the simple "Eskimo" people to hate the British and cut off contact with the civilized people. His sympathy for oppressed nations and his passion for hating imperialism are fully revealed in the picture.

That's right, he is a progressive humanist, and he has a liberal worldview. In this film, even if it is sentimental, he ultimately and greatly unfolds the suffering of the oppressed nations. Who are the barbarians? Please think about it.

To say it again, before a further understanding, all he can do is humanitarian sentimentality. When he finally used the method used by Griffith in "Broken Blossoms" with extremely painful capital letters, he made Mala escape in the snow. Without food, after killing all the family dogs, he fought with the wild wolves again. In order to escape the white man's gallows, he had no choice but to drift with the waves on the melting ice floes with his wife, even to the point of never knowing where they would end up. This sad and painful poetic sentiment undoubtedly deeply stimulated the audience's hearts. Therefore, in terms of directing techniques, the most successful is the grasp of the tone. As for the cleanliness of the picture, the delicacy of each love scene, and the tension of the hunting scene, it can be said to be wonderful to the extreme. Does anyone still think that the mother breastfeeding or Mala's second wife singing bare-breasted is lewd "sensationalism" or "eroticism"? He is good at handling the sound of sound films in the wind, the wailing of dogs on cold nights,... This can be seen here. As for several "Eskimo" actors, such as the male lead who played Mala and the two female leads, they all performed extremely well, especially the male lead when he broke free from the iron chains and when he and his second wife sang in the hut; even more showing the genius of the performance. It is said that these two people have been taken back to Hollywood by Mr. Van Dyke.

In short, this is a very valuable film. I hereby introduce it to the readers.

Review of "Blood Money" 175

— Luo Ping

Blood Money | Nanjing |

"Broadway Bill" is rough, vivid, and has a kind of unrestrained momentum. Although it consciously promotes the imperialist war of aggression, we can see the reality of the lower class society in the United States from it.

"Blood Money" is elegant and ordinary. It describes a love story in a leisurely tone. However, the so-called exposure of the lower class life, apart from some hula dances and decadent music in the nightclub at the beginning, simply cannot see anything.

However, we must admit that there are indeed giants of the lower class society like Bairac in the United States.

He is a rogue who associates with government officials and specializes in bond guarantees for others. His life is playing with women, playing dog racing, and playing golf. He is completely an idler.

Another kind of character is Turell, who specializes in major cases of thieves, but we cannot tell from his appearance.

We cannot find fundamentally different social backgrounds from Bairac and Turell. They are all upper class members of the modern urban lumpenproletariat. Therefore, we can only see their elegant and enjoyable life in "Blood Money," not their rough and wandering life.

However, the love lan ling in "Blood Money" is even more worthy of our attention.

The development of American capitalism has reached a point of extreme maturity, and all social upward mobility and progress have stopped, and we can only see its signs of decline, death, and decay, although we should particularly point out a new and energetic factor that is growing there.

The life of the powerful in modern society has therefore reached the highest point of decadence, ordinariness, and ugliness, so the greatest need of all is extraordinary stimulation, and fantasy and curiosity are popular in that lifeless social group.

The emancipation of women in modern society was originally incomplete, but now, women under the deformed social system can no longer be satisfied with sexual pleasure and all other high-level and elegant pleasures, so they have further developed curiosity and fantasy. In the United States, the criteria for women to choose a husband even abandon gentlemen and turn to rogues, which is nothing more than an essence of this phenomenon.

The love lan ling is such a woman. From here, we can see the degree of corruption in American society, and the inevitability of the growth and abandonment of this old society by new factors - although the playwright of "Blood Money" will not understand this.

Among the actors, George Bancroft, who left the "film circle" a year ago because he was unhappy with making films that he didn't want to act in, has now rejoined 20th Century Fox. Because of his willingness, what we see on the screen also feels that he is indeed working hard.

The director's technique uses a lot of "crossing," and his messiness is always a little bit undisguised and felt by us.

Film Novel

Empress Catherine SearletEmpress 176

— Su Mei

Alexei then presented gifts, giving Sophia winter clothing for use in the north, and to Johanna, a portrait of the Russian Empress, inlaid with jewels. Johanna thanked the ambassador on the one hand, and on the other, feeling somewhat annoyed by Sophia's silence, signaled for her to speak. Sophia's rosy face flushed red, and looking at the portrait of the Russian Empress, she asked Alexei, "Did you not bring a portrait of the crown prince?" Duke Alexei laughed and said, "Do you want him to be more handsome than all other men?" Sophia, appearing somewhat embarrassed, said, "Isn't that so?" Alexei said, "Very well, the crown prince is exactly as you hope, or even better. He has a tall stature, like a Greek god. His eyes are as blue as the clear sky, and his hair is as lustrous as ebony. His strength can rival a team of oxen. He is now neglecting food and sleep while waiting for you." Although the Duke spoke eloquently, his eyes seemed to be covered by a layer of black纱, concealing some secret. Sophia's mother instructed her to withdraw, so she politely thanked Alexei and withdrew. As she reached the door, she hesitated for a moment, turned her head, and glanced at the ambassador who had come from afar. Her heart pounded like a startled goose as she rushed upstairs to her bedroom. Once in her room, she took out her 洋囡囡 (foreign doll). She whispered to it, "Sophia Friederike, are you happy? You are getting married, you will have a man. I am your Russian husband, a great Russian Grand Duke, the crown prince. We will be married soon." After she finished speaking, she silently pondered. She immediately felt a sense of dread, causing her brow to furrow. She would be leaving her family, … leaving her beloved father, … leaving her mother, who would certainly return to Prussia after the wedding ceremony, … her nanny Kadul, … her professor Wagner, … and all the life she knew and was accustomed to, … to go to that distant north, a foreign, cold land, … she then thought of the fur coats and hot water bottles, etc., sent by the Russian ambassador, and she felt a chill.
